The foreign goods industry, including Wang Renfa, Zhongxi, Zhongfa, Luo Yuanxing, Gongshengkui, Cha Yushun, and several other shops, suffered a total loss of over 300,000 yuan. There were many other losses of four or five thousand yuan, which cannot be detailed. (November 30th)

Zhang Xueliang's Remarks After Arriving in Tianjin 73

Excellent Impressions of the Trip to the Capital

Post-War Reconstruction in the Northwest is Easy to Begin

Tianjin Correspondence: Vice Commander Zhang Xueliang participated in the Fourth Plenary Session during this trip to Beijing and provided much support for the plan to reorganize the situation in the North. In the past twenty-odd days, the situation in the North has gradually stabilized. With Wang, Yan, and Feng successively leaving Shanxi, military and political affairs can be gradually reorganized. However, the four northeastern provinces have complex administrative affairs. Due to the inconvenience of Acting Governor Zhang Zuoxiang making independent decisions on many important policies, he repeatedly telegraphed the central government to request Zhang's return to the north quickly. Zhang departed from Beijing on the 5th of this month and arrived in Tianjin by special train at 7:30 AM on the 6th. In addition to the people who accompanied him, Chairman Chiang specifically dispatched Liu Guang, Director of the First Bureau of the General Staff, and Gao Lingbai, Secretary of the National Government, to escort him to Tianjin. The Tianjin military and political authorities had already begun preparations to welcome Zhang. Both the East and West railway stations were decorated with colorful arches, adorned with welcoming words, and illuminated with electric lights in the evening, creating a very brilliant atmosphere. The inside of the stations was also extensively decorated with electric and gas lights, creating the atmosphere of a city that never sleeps. Welcoming personnel were assigned specific positions. White lines were drawn on the platforms to ensure that everyone stood within the lines, and powdered signs were erected with the names of the organizations and groups, so that they could stand in their respective places and avoid disorder. Security within the stations was handled by the public security bureau's security team and soldiers from the 25th Brigade stationed in Tianjin. The area from the North Exit of the Japanese Concession to outside the West Station, and from the Jingang Bridge of the French Concession to outside the East Station, was guarded by a sentry monitoring pedestrians every ten steps, but traffic was not completely cut off. Hebei Chairman Wang Shuchang, Directors Lin Chengxiu, Chang Bingyi, Ke Yufang, Yao Hong, Zhang Jian'an, Wang Yuke, Mayor Zang Qifang, and various bureau chiefs, customs supervisors Han Linsheng, Hong Weiguo, Wang Shouchong, and other important figures took special trains that evening to Machang, where they met Zhang in person to discuss important political matters. The other welcoming organizations and groups, numbering about three hundred people, greeted him at the East and West railway stations. At 5:10, the vanguard arrived, and Zhang's special train arrived at the West Station at 7:30, stopping briefly before departing. He got off the train at the East Station and took a car to his private residence in the concession. Those who were welcoming also rushed to the residence to pay their respects. The gatekeeper said that the Vice Commander was resting temporarily due to fatigue from the journey and would not be able to receive guests until 3:00 PM in the afternoon. The people then dispersed. At 5:00 PM that afternoon, the reporter visited Zhang at his residence. Zhang said that he had gained excellent impressions from his trip to Beijing. The central authorities are very motivated and take responsibility for everything. Chairman Chiang has a strong spirit and is determined to govern the country well, with genuine sincerity. China is a vast and complex society, and there are many difficulties in everything. It is inevitable that a small number of elements cannot be completely satisfactory, but overall, it cannot but be considered satisfactory. Chiang has recently been receptive to advice, such as the preparatory convocation of the National Assembly, the reorganization of party organizations, and the recruitment and employment of talented people outside the party, all of which are the result of adopting dissenting opinions from various parties. From now on, if we can cooperate with one heart and one mind and govern together, the country's future will be truly promising. The reporter asked about the post-war reconstruction in the Northwest. Zhang said that since Yan and Feng have already left, there will be no problems in starting the post-war reconstruction. Shanxi's affairs will be handled by Shang Zhen. Given a reasonable amount of time, things will gradually get on track. Military affairs will be easier to arrange. The reporter asked if the Vice Commander wanted to meet with Yan Xishan. Zhang said that if Mr. Yan wanted to meet, he would have no objections. If he comes to visit, he will be received. Finally, the reporter further asked whether the finances and transportation of the Northeast would be entirely managed by the central government. Zhang said that not only the Northeast, but all of the North should be under a unified government. However, the local authorities should of course also have the power and responsibility to manage and propose. For example, the Northeast Transportation Committee will not be abolished, which is the meaning of this. As a result of the abolition of the likin tax, local revenues have sharply decreased, so all military and administrative expenses of local governments should be transferred from the central government's revenue. If there is a shortfall, the central government will assist. If there is a surplus, it will be handed over to the central government. This is the common practice of finance in various countries. Zhang said that he was particularly pleased with this trip, first, because it was decided that the likin tax would be abolished on January 1st of next year without further delay, which would have a positive impact on the national economy, and second, because the negotiations with Russia were also making progress. At this point, the reporter excused himself. He met Zhu Guangmu, who said that party affairs in the Northeast were already being prepared. After Qiang returns, he will lead all military personnel to join the party. Local party branches will also begin to be organized. Zhang is about to return to Shenyang because Zhang Zuoxiang is eager to return to Jilin to handle provincial affairs. Zhang will enter the customs again after Liaoning's affairs are completed, because there is nothing that must be done in Peiping at this time, so he will not go to Peiping. It is said that Zhang plans to leave the customs in three or four days. (December 7th)

Korean Residents in Andong Smuggling and Committing Violence 74

Japanese Police Protect Illegal Korean Residents

Assaulting and Arresting Customs Officers

Shenyang Correspondence: Andong County is a large station on the South Manchurian Railway, with a prosperous market and abundant production. It also has so-called attached areas, where many Japanese and Korean residents live. Therefore, the diplomatic situation is more complicated than in other inland areas. On the 28th of last month, a case occurred in which Korean residents gathered to destroy the Jiangqiao branch of our country's customs office and assaulted our customs officers. Negotiations have not yet been resolved to this day. Unexpectedly, at 6:00 AM on the 2nd of this month, about thirty Korean residents, each holding wooden sticks and carrying smuggled goods in their waists, arrived at the customs checkpoint. Seeing customs officers conducting inspections, the Korean residents attempted to rush through, swarming forward and surrounding the customs officers, subjecting them to verbal abuse and insults. At the time, Ding of Patrol Team No. 7 was seriously injured. Afterwards, the Korean residents left triumphantly. Unexpectedly, one wave subsided, and another wave rose. At around 8:00 PM that evening, four more Korean residents, each carrying several catties of copper coins, crossed the customs gate from Jiangqiao and passed behind the Japanese bridge-guarding police station, hoping to smuggle them. This was seen by a patrol team who stepped forward to stop them. The four Korean residents, seeing that they had been exposed, scattered and fled. Three of them escaped, leaving only one behind. Ninety catties of copper coins were found in his waist. At the time, the Japanese police were on the scene, turning a blind eye and not stopping them. When the Korean resident became anxious and bit a patrolman, the patrolman used legitimate defense to resist with the wooden stick he was carrying. Unexpectedly, the Japanese police immediately stepped forward, grabbed the patrolman, and used extreme violence. After negotiations with the officer on duty, they not only ignored him but were also extremely barbaric, using both fists and feet. As a result, the patrol team was arrested by the Japanese police and detained at the headquarters. Since these two incidents occurred, all Chinese officers of the Andong Customs Outer Bureau believe that the Japanese are instigating Korean residents to make things difficult for the customs, and that if this continues, the consequences will be dire. Personnel from various branches in the Japanese Concession agreed to go on strike to show their resistance, await a resolution through negotiations, and issued a declaration on the 4th, sending it to various provinces in Northeast China to raise public awareness. The declaration stated: "Japanese imperialists, wielding unequal treaties as a talisman and consular jurisdiction as a tool, with military force as a backing, using the concession as a breeding ground for evil, protecting tax evasion, and doing their utmost to insult our administrative personnel. Our customs personnel, concerned with our national revenue and their duties, cannot sit idly by against the tax evasion of Japanese and Korean residents. The Japanese authorities are indulging these fierce and unruly elements, carrying out assaults and insults at will, resulting in customs officers Zhang Chengming, Yu Luomin, Yu Chuanjie, Wang Huachun, Wang Guofan, and others being seriously injured one after another. They have also instigated Korean residents to destroy the customs office, with He Jun Jiayu almost being drowned in the Yalu River, and Guard Yang Shuqi being beaten nearly to death. Although the customs authorities have negotiated with them in many ways, they not only ignore them but also intensify their efforts, interfering in our administration by force and insulting our staff. Customs officers Xie Guodong, Guan Guangyan, Wu Jingwen, Yu Chuanjie, Lin Wanzhi, Chen Weitao, Zhou Maoxu, and others have been unreasonably detained and abused by the Japanese police station. As if that were not enough, they have incited Korean residents to attack our branches every night, and the lives of our customs officers on duty are often in danger. At around 6:00 PM on the 2nd of this month, Wang Yuecheng, a guard of our customs, was beaten by Korean residents at the Iron Bridge branch for suppressing smuggling. The Japanese police did not ask right or wrong, but arrested the guard and took him to the police station, tying him up with ropes and using both fists and feet, beating him for more than two hours, resulting in injuries all over his body. Our inspector and customs officer Guan Guangyan went to reason with them, but was also insulted and driven away. Such ferocity, barbarity, and disregard for the law is outrageous and infuriating. We, the undersigned, are unable to perform our duties and our lives are in danger and without protection. Therefore, as a last resort, we are temporarily going on strike at all branches in the Japanese Concession, awaiting negotiations by the authorities. Fearing that the outside world does not understand the true situation, we hereby issue this declaration." After receiving the above declaration, various popular groups and national diplomacy associations in Shenyang were indignant at the Japanese protecting Korean residents and acting lawlessly. They are currently discussing ways to respond. (December 7th)

The Full Text of the Civil Code, Book of Relatives (5) (Continued) 75

(Article 1094) If both parents are unable to exercise or bear the rights and obligations towards their minor children, or if the parents die without a will designating a guardian, the guardian shall be determined in the following order: (1) Grandparents living with the minor; (2) Head of the household; (3) Grandparents not living with the minor; (4) Paternal uncle or uncle; (5) A person selected by the family council. (Article 1095) A person who becomes a guardian according to the provisions of the preceding article may not resign from their position without legitimate reasons. (Article 1096) Minors and persons under interdiction shall not be guardians. (Article 1097) Unless otherwise provided, the guardian shall, within the scope of protecting and promoting the interests of the ward, exercise and bear the rights and obligations of parents towards their minor children, but in the case of temporary entrustment by the parents, only to the extent of the entrusted duties. (Article 1098) The guardian shall be the legal representative of the ward. (Article 1099) At the commencement of guardianship, the guardian shall, together with the person designated by the family council, draw up an inventory of the ward's property. (Article 1100) The ward's property shall be managed by the guardian, and the management expenses shall be borne by the ward's property. The guardian shall manage the ward's property with the same care as managing their own affairs. (Article 1101) The guardian shall not use or dispose of the ward's property for purposes other than the ward's benefit. When disposing of real property, the permission of the family council shall also be obtained. (Article 1102) The guardian shall not acquire the ward's property. (Article 1103) The guardian shall report the status of the ward's property to the family council in detail at least once a year. (Article 1104) The guardian may request remuneration, the amount of which shall be determined by the family council based on their labor and the income status of the ward's property. (Article 1105) The provisions of Articles 1101 and 1103 to 1106 shall not apply when the grandparents living with the minor are the guardians. (Article 1106) In any of the following circumstances, the family council may remove the guardian: (1) Violation of legal obligations; (2) Lack of ability to pay; (3) Violation of the instructions of the family council by the guardian selected by the family council. (Article 1107) When the guardianship relationship terminates, the guardian shall immediately, together with the person designated by the family council, liquidate the property and transfer the property to the new guardian. If the ward has reached adulthood, it shall be returned to the ward. If the ward dies, it shall be returned to their heirs. The guardian shall not be released from their responsibility until the family council has approved the results of the aforementioned liquidation. (Article 1108) In the event of the guardian's death, the liquidation under the preceding article shall be carried out by their heirs. (Article 1109) The right to claim compensation for damages caused by the guardian to the ward's property shall be extinguished if it is not exercised within two years from the time the family council rejects the liquidation result. Section 2: Guardianship of Persons Under Interdiction (Article 1110) A person under interdiction shall have a guardian. (Article 1111) The guardian of a person under interdiction shall be determined in the following order: (1) Spouse; (2) Parents; (3) Grandparents living with the person under interdiction; (4) Head of the household; (5) A person designated by the deceased father or mother in a will. If the guardian cannot be determined according to the provisions of the preceding paragraph, the court shall consult the opinion of the family council and select one. (Article 1112) The guardian shall, for the benefit of the ward, care for and treat their body according to the ward's financial situation. If the guardian sends the ward to a mental hospital or confines them in a private residence, the consent of the family council shall be obtained, but this shall not apply when the parents or grandparents living with the person under interdiction are the guardians. (Article 1113) The guardianship of persons under interdiction shall, unless otherwise provided in this section, mutatis mutandis apply to the provisions regarding the guardianship of minors. The provisions of Articles 1101 and 1103 to 1106 shall also not apply when the parents are the guardians. (To be continued)

Fengxian 78

The Old and New Committees of the Relief Institute Have Not Completed the Takeover. The County Relief Preparatory Committee, due to its ineffectiveness, was reorganized by a resolution of the Provisional Local Council, and the County Government separately appointed committee members to re-establish the committee. The old preparatory committee refused to recognize the process as illegal and declared to the County Government that it had separately telegraphed the Ministry of Interior and the Provincial Government for instructions and would only comply with them. Before receiving clear instructions, it would be inappropriate to transfer the work without authorization, thus violating the legal process. The County Government, upon receiving the report, immediately issued an order on the 3rd reprimanding them not to resist and cause inconvenience. Therefore, the new committee side yesterday dispatched Chairman Ruan Xiyao, accompanied by committee member Zhuang Qingqi, etc., to take over. Because the committee did not send anyone to contact them, they inquired about the handling of the matter yesterday. They were instructed that the case had been resolved by the Local Council and had been approved with a record, so the committee could not refuse to hand over the work on the pretext of it not being authorized. The Chairman, etc., should be responsible for going to take over the work. If they truly refused to hand over the work, they should report it for review and seizure. The new committee has re-scheduled the takeover date and has requested the County Supervisory Committee to send personnel to assist in the handling of the matter. It is not known whether the result will be satisfactory.

Wuxi 80

Two Pig Boats Robbed at the Same Time. Liu Renbao, a partner of the Hongchang Pig Company outside Suzhou's Lümen, recently took money to the Yongtaichang Pig Company in Lücheng and bought more than 30 pigs, hiring Zhao Ada's barge to transport them to Suzhou. At about 9:00 PM the day before yesterday, while passing through the Qiganbang estuary near Xin'an Town in the 12th District (Xin'an Township) of the county, four bandit boats suddenly appeared, and more than a dozen bandits armed with pistols, flashlights, and other weapons shouted to stop. The bandits swarmed onto the boat and searched and robbed at will. After about an hour, they returned to their original boat with their loot and fled quickly. Upon inspection, it was found that six large pigs and five yuan in cash had been robbed. At the same time, a pig boat from Jiangbei was also robbed in the same place, and two pigs were stolen.

A City Gate Added to the Jixiang Bridge Embankment. The First District Party Department of the county held its fifth committee meeting yesterday and resolved that the city wall of the county, which had previously been ordered to be temporarily suspended from demolition, was causing traffic jams and economic depression. As a temporary solution, a city gate should be added to the Jixiang Bridge Embankment to boost the market and facilitate traffic. It was resolved to report the case to the County Party Consolidation Committee and forward it to the County Government for handling. The Autonomous Research Association Asks for Financial Assistance. Since its establishment, the Township Autonomous Research Association of the First District (Wuxi City) has been suffering from financial difficulties, which has prevented it from carrying out its work to the fullest extent. Recently, the association sent a letter to the Municipal Property Management Committee requesting an annual subsidy of 360 yuan to facilitate its work. After receiving the letter, the Municipal Committee stated that whether private groups or organizations could receive public subsidies was not explicitly stipulated by law. It inquired with the County Government on how to handle the situation and requested instructions to be followed.

Tao Xiaodi Lights Candles to Apologize. Tao Xiaodi, the owner of the Dafeng Cigarette and Paper Shop at the entrance of Neisi Lane in the city, recently secretly set up a gambling den on the upper floor of his shop, with huge amounts of money being won and lost. At about 8:00 PM yesterday, just as the gambling den was in full swing, someone heard the noise and tried to enter, but Tao Xiaodi blocked him and did not allow him to go upstairs. He also beat the person severely. Unable to defeat the crowd, the person immediately took a deck of mahjong tiles and ran to report to the police officer on duty. Later, after Lu Zhonglian intervened to mediate, Tao Xiaodi lit incense and candles in the nearby Caishen Temple to apologize, and the matter was settled.

Jiangyin 82

The Manager of Junda Pawnshop Summoned to Court. Jiangyin Qingyang Town's Junda Pawnshop was established by the Sheng family of Changzhou in the twelfth year of the Tongzhi reign of the Qing Dynasty. The capital was silver ingots. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, it was converted to 34,482.758 yuan. Since the Republic of China, it has suffered losses year after year. In the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, during the Qi-Lu dispute, it lost 18,704.22 yuan. This spring, the pawnshop's manager, Jiang Xiangxian, and the silver room manager, Cao Zhifu, colluded to commit fraud. In the sale of silk cocoons, it lost as much as 70,000 to 80,000 yuan, making it impossible to maintain business operations. Gold and silver jewelry were taken by Shen Jinqing, the owner of Shen Changyuan Rice Shop on North Street in the town, as collateral for advances. Jiang Xiangxian and Cao Zhifu remained outside, avoiding the pawnshop. The Jiangyin and Wuxi pawnshops organized a debt group to clean up the pawnshop. The shareholders also hired lawyer Zhuang Zenghu to file a civil lawsuit with the Jiangyin County Government. After the court session on the 9th, because Jiang Xiangxian and Cao Zhifu were both in Shanghai, the leader of the detective team, Yang Bingwei, and the judicial police chief, Wu Bowen, prepared documents and came to Shanghai to submit them to the Special Zone Court, requesting that Jiang and Cao be summoned to Cheng for interrogation to determine whether there was any fraud and the specific amount of the loss so that it could be recovered.

Last month, County Magistrate Li, together with Commander Yang of the Fortress, dispatched police squad leader Li Zhaoming and special agent Ji Yongxiang to arrest Chen Bingquan, Liu Hanbing, and others, former water police subordinates of He Zhanao, in the Huangtiangang River for transporting opium. After a military trial in the county, they were escorted to the Provincial Government the day before yesterday and sent to the Zhenjiang Local Court for interrogation. After investigation by Prosecutor Zhu, Liu Hanbing and Pan Rongfu were detained, Chen Bingquan, Zhang Yulin, Qiu Zanqing, Chen Changfa, and Li Weiqing were released on bail, and Pan Bingsheng and Xu Luotang were released. Because a hearing was scheduled, a letter was sent to the Jiangyin County Government to summon Li Zhaoming and Li Yongxiang to the Zhenjiang Court for questioning. Yesterday, the bailiff went to summon them, but Li Zhaoming had already left the police team and his whereabouts were unknown, so he could not be summoned.

Xu Zukang Granted Bail. Cao Xiangfang, the head of the Fifth District Security Regiment, reported the arrest of Xu Zukang. A group of people from the area jointly petitioned the county government to protect him. On the 8th, the county government summoned everyone for questioning. Chen Shaorong, the squad leader of the Security Regiment, stated that he saw a dark shadow near the wall while on patrol on the evening of the 29th and captured Xu Zukang, finding a slogan on him. Xu said that he was falsely accused of being arrested on the 30th. Shi Yuanzheng stated that Xu was not captured on the morning of the 30th. Zhou Chunlin, the owner of a tea shop, stated that Cao, the head of the regiment, was drinking tea in the shop on the morning of the 30th and that Xu was brought in by several members of the regiment. Fang Ziqing, Chen Jinxi, Wu Zhenming, and Liu Neigen, the tenant, all stated that Xu Zukang was arrested on the morning of the 30th. Xu Zukang stated that it was completely Cao's retaliation for private revenge, abusing his power, etc. After the interrogation, he was temporarily granted bail pending further interrogation.

Xiaoshan 87

1.2 Million Yuan Allocated for Xiaochang Road. The Xiaochang Road project is very urgent. The cost of purchasing materials for the road is more than 1.6 million yuan. In addition to the 400,000 yuan that has already been paid and the allocation of construction bonds and special construction donations, another 1.2 million yuan has been borrowed from the Bank of China to start construction.

Businessmen and Citizens Request Removal of Police Subsidy Donation. Xiaoshan's police expenses have always been insufficient. After discussion at the County Government Meeting, it was decided that tea houses and restaurants would be taxed monthly according to the size of their business to subsidize police expenses, and each public security bureau was ordered to investigate and register each household and compile a list to begin collecting taxes. It is reported that more than 60 liquor merchants in Dongxiang, including Qianhesheng, have stated that their business has been difficult to support in recent years and that the additional donation will be too difficult to bear. They have jointly submitted detailed reports to the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments requesting the county to revoke the order to maintain business operations.

Dai Jitao's Telegram to Teachers and Students in Guangdong 89

Hoping for Shared Virtue and Common Belief in the University,

Unanimously Welcoming Principal Jin's Swift Assumption of Office

President Dai, Chairman of the Board of Guangzhou Sun Yat-sen University, telegraphed the school's faculty and students yesterday, saying: "To Director Shen Pengfei of Guangzhou Sun Yat-sen University and all faculty, staff, and students: Your telegrams received. I have heard that recently, university students have been unsettled and full of discussions due to the change of university president. Hearing this from afar, I deeply regret that our school is a university personally founded by the Premier and the only institution of higher learning in the South. After many twists and turns, it has finally stabilized. For the past three years, the faculty, staff, and all students have shared virtues and worked together, each pursuing their studies. The excellent academic atmosphere is praised throughout the country. Now that the overall situation is settled, all construction should be actively pursued. For the various construction projects of our school, it will not be successful without someone focusing on responsibility. The Central Government has repeatedly resolved that the university president cannot concurrently hold other positions. Chuanxian repeatedly declined positions in the Central Government, but was not permitted. Therefore, on one hand, I suggested to the Central Government to establish a university board of directors to assume responsibility for construction, and on the other hand, I requested the Central Government to appoint President Zhu to be in charge of university administration. Recently, with the resignation of the president of the Central University, it was decided to transfer President Zhu to Beijing. Regarding the selection of a candidate for our school, after repeated deliberations and with the unanimous approval of the board members in Beijing, Mr. Jin Xiangfan was appointed as the president. Mr. Xiangfan is an advanced member of our party, and his contributions to education in Guangdong are deeply appreciated by the Central Government. If he can devote himself wholeheartedly to the university, all future construction will surely follow the Premier's will and continue the established direction with effort. Chuanxian and other board members will do their best to assist him, hoping for its completion. The most important thing at present is that the faculty, staff, and students should share virtues and unite in one heart, unanimously obeying the Central Government's orders and President Jin's guidance. You must know that the government and the board of directors are more thoughtful about the university's future than the students, and their responsibility for the university's future is also more practical than the students'. The students must not listen to rumors and create suspicions to destroy the established good academic atmosphere and endanger the university's future construction. I deeply hope that you will understand this and, with a spirit of kinship, uphold the common belief in the university and unanimously welcome President Jin's swift assumption of office. Not only will the comrades in the Central Government be at ease, but the new bright future of the university will also be further advanced from this point. I will wait until my official duties are slightly more free and will definitely return to the school with Director Sun Zhesheng at the end of the year and the beginning of the year to jointly plan the construction project of the new school building. Words cannot express everything, please understand. Chuanxian respectfully kowtows."

Elementary School Party Doctrine Speech Competition 91

—Today's Second Group Preliminary—

The First Group's Preliminary Was Held Yesterday

Five Winning Members Were Selected

The city's elementary school Party Doctrine speech competition was convened by the Municipal Training Department at 1:00 PM yesterday in the auditorium on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. More than 300 people attended, including representatives from 20 schools and audience members. The meeting started on time, presided over by Jiang Tanshu. The situation was very grand. The second group will be convened at 1:00 PM this afternoon to continue the preliminary. Details are recorded as follows:

Arrangement of the Venue: The Municipal Training Department arranged the venue in advance. The two large characters "Listen Attentively" were hung on the stage, followed by the words "Shanghai Elementary School Student Party Doctrine Speech Competition, First Group". The venue order was quite solemn and orderly. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, representatives from various schools and listeners arrived one after another, full of energy. First, lots were drawn to determine the order of speeches, and then the preliminary began as scheduled. The judges all adopted anonymous methods according to the lot numbers to ensure fairness.

Chairman's Report: Briefly stated, today's Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters Training Department's elementary school Party Doctrine speech competition is an initiative. The mission of the Training Department is to deeply root the Three Principles of the People in the hearts of the masses, and training elementary school students is a fundamental method. For example, if you want a tree to have tight branches and lush leaves, the cultivation of its roots and wood still requires attention to sowing and sprouting. Therefore, training elementary school students is very important. The holding of this Party Doctrine speech competition, on the one hand, promotes the development of the Three Principles of the People, and on the other hand, enables elementary school students to have a deeper understanding of Party Doctrine. Although all elementary schools have a Party Doctrine course, they are perfunctory and cannot be completely without process. After this competition, the excellent ones will know to work harder, and the inferior ones will know to be more vigilant. Then the development of Party Doctrine education can have a new motivation from this point. Therefore, this elementary school Party Doctrine speech competition held by the Municipal Training Department is of great importance, and so on.

Names of Winning Members: The performances of all participants in yesterday's preliminary were excellent. However, due to the limited number of places, only five were selected: first (Bide) Zhang Hesheng, second (Jiancheng) Xu Zhenyu, third (Shangwen) Jiang Derong, fourth (Meixi) Zhou Zengye, fifth (Suzhou Luhai) Xu Meichi. The judges were Wu Xianren, Zhou Yingcai, Zhou Shang, and Li Zheng. The chief judge was Jiang Huaisu.

Today's Preliminary: Today's second preliminary will be held. The list is as follows: Liuyun, (Zhu Zishen) Xunyu, (Shao Runlin) Aiqun (Liu Fubao) Minzhi, (Zhang Wei) Nanqu (Zhao Ruying) Gaochang (Wu Gen) Yucai, (Shen Yiding) Mingde, (Liu Ruonan) Yangzheng, (Zhu Jiwu) Wuzou, (Xiong Minghui) Huabao (Ye Junhui) Shanggong (Jiang Douliang) Motang, (Jia Shanren) Qingxin (Cen Liren) Cangji, (Bu Shugan) Chengze, (Li Changhua) Meilan, (Mei Hongyun) Guangzhao Girls' Elementary, (Ma Xuemin) Qiujiang, (Yan Jinfa) Chaozong, (Zhang Runlin) Yongxing, (Xiao Yushu) It is also heard that the judges for today's preliminary are Cheng Kuanzheng, (Principal of Municipal Wusong Public School) Jishi, (Former Chief of the Party Member Training Section of the Zhejiang Provincial Training Department) Yan Wenwei, (Director of Moral Education of Minli Middle School) Zhou Hanmei, (Chief of the Guidance Section of the Municipal Propaganda Department) The preliminary chairman and judge is Jiang Huaisu.

Zhang Yuejun and Others Host a Banquet to Raise Funds for the Capital Women's College 92

Yesterday at noon, Zhang Yuejun, Niu Yangsheng, Jiao Yitang, Wang Yiting, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai and others hosted a banquet at Jue Lin to solicit construction funds for the Capital Women's Law College. More than 40 people attended, including Zhao Jinqing, Mei WanHua, Wen Lanting, Wu Zhihao, Xu Weizhen, Wang Fengqing, Wang Jingqi, Wang Hongpang, Madam Niu, Madam Jiao, and Ms. Bao. Niu Yongjian stood up to give a speech, briefly saying that the National Government, based on the principle of equality between men and women established by the Premier, is earnestly seeking its realization. The Legislative Yuan recently formulated the Civil Code, based on this purpose. Therefore, in law, women have completely obtained equal status. However, in order for women to exercise equal rights, they must have considerable political and legal knowledge. The comrades founded the Capital Women's Law College to cultivate such talents. Now there is a base, and active progress is being made. However, the construction of the college buildings still requires huge funds. The comrades are weak and have to rely on the great strength and enthusiasm of the gentlemen in Shanghai to help. Next, Mayor Zhang spoke, briefly saying that the Capital Women's Law College was founded to promote national women's political and legal education. Therefore, we cannot regard it as a business in a corner of the capital. However, Shanghai has too many undertakings to handle. Almost all kinds of charitable construction projects everywhere come to talk to us, asking for help. However, some powerful people in Shanghai are unwilling to come out, and we cannot see them. The people who are willing to come out are always these few people. Sometimes it really feels too much to handle, and some people inevitably feel annoyed. In fact, we are in this position, and people from all sides trust us and ask us for help. We are very honored and should not feel annoyed. We were just talking about Bodhisattvas. We can say that we are like Bodhisattvas. For all kinds of requests from all sides, we should always do our best to satisfy their wishes. Taking advantage of this opportunity today, I will say a little meaning, hoping that the gentlemen present will tell those who are unwilling to come out that it is a very valuable thing in life to be requested by all parties. Today, Mr. Mei WanHua and Mr. Tan Wang have all come. After the contract of the Grand Stage is completed, they will perform charity shows for our Women's Law College, raising funds with artistic contributions. It must be more and easier than the donations we are soliciting now. Then, Yu Qiaqing, Jiao Yitang, Wang Xiaolai and other gentlemen spoke one after another, and the atmosphere was extremely pleasant. When the bell rang three times, they dispersed with joy. It is reported that the construction costs were separately recognized by those who arrived, and the funds donated were not small.

Shanghai Basketball League 96

Registration Begins Immediately

The Shanghai Basketball League competition, sponsored by the Chinese National Sports Association, is scheduled to begin on January 3, 1931. The registration procedures and competition highlights are listed below: (1) Old members can register from now until the 20th. When registering, please collect the player registration form.

(2) New members are limited to ten teams. These ten teams will be based on the order of registration. (Registration must be accompanied by a formal request letter from now on) Additions to old members, even those in Group B, are also considered new members but do not have to pay membership fees.

(3) This year's membership fee for new members is ten yuan, and the registration fee is five yuan per team.

(2) Three protests in the league. (A) The Beicheng team protested that the Dajiang team used the names of players who had not joined the competition on the match report. The matter was proven. The Dajiang team should forfeit the match and be given a warning. (B) The Anglo-American team protested that the referee's decision was improper. It was resolved to ask the referee to provide a detailed report of the match for further processing. (C) Yaxiyia protested that the Zhendan B team used a player who had used someone else's name to join the competition and used the names of players who had not joined the competition to replace the names of players on the match report. After various parties proved that the protest was true, the Zhendan team cheated for profit, violating the spirit of sports. In addition to forfeiting the match with the Yaxiyia team, they were also penalized with a fine of five yuan. It was also decided that if such cases of impersonation are found in the future, the team will be immediately suspended from the entire season's competition to maintain the spirit of the league.

Jiaotong University's Hegemony Reborn 106

The Jiaotong University football team has always been known for its elite and invincible strength, holding the top position in Shanghai. In recent years, its star players have scattered, and its strength has declined. Only in the recent battles with Fudan and Guangfu Central have there been special improvements. It is thought that the Jiaotong University's hegemony will have a trend of rebirth. Jiaotong University uses strong men to occupy various internal positions, so as to prevent the invasion of powerful enemies. The five external forwards are agile and quick. Every time they gain momentum, the five routes advance, and the defenders are always confused and do not know where to follow. With internal strength and external sharpness, able to attack and defend, the future of Jiaotong University is truly unlimited.

Central University Trapped in Wetlands 107

The Central University football team has excellent qualifications and can be trained. Coach Jin plans to conquer Hangzhou, Shanghai, and Suzhou to increase the team's experience. Yesterday, the team suffered a great blow from Jiaotong University because they were not accustomed to wetland warfare. However, the activity of its two wings and the solidity of the goalkeeper added color to the team. The biggest weakness is that the external forwards and internal guards cannot unite as one. Perhaps the field was muddy and slippery, making it inconvenient to advance and retreat, causing heroes to have no place to use their abilities.

Zhang Jingyong Makes the First Contribution 110

The mobilization order was issued, and the fierce battle began. Jiaotong University passed the ball three or four times and passed it to Fei Fuxu's feet. He picked it up out of thin air and crossed it in front of the goal from the crowd. Both sides' soldiers missed it. Jiaotong University's Liu Ximeng and Xue Wenxiu shot one after another, but none of them hit the target. The ball's momentum turned and a storm arose in front of Jiaotong University's goal. There was a melee within five steps for a long time, but Jiaotong University did not lose the goal, which was fortunate. Before long, Jiaotong University launched a counterattack and shot many times, but it was either blocked by the internal guards or blocked by the goalkeeper. After a long time, in the last five minutes, Zhang Jingyong headed the ball in. In the first half, Jiaotong University took the lead with one to zero.

Jiaotong University's Aggressive Momentum 111

In the second half, Jiaotong University's overly active forwards scattered the enemy everywhere, so they took the lead and were always on the offensive. Central University also made some progress in the first ten minutes, but Jiaotong University's Wang Gongchen, with his strong feet and calm attitude, dominated the rear, coupled with the cooperation of the forwards and the stability of the goalkeeper, Central University's several attacks all ended in failure. From then on, Jiaotong University's athletes were often seen in the Central University area, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, feinting to the east and attacking the west, and encircling from the left and right. Central University's heavy troops held the defense and maintained it with hard work. After ten battles and ten rounds, they were unable to break through. Central University suddenly broke out of the encirclement and launched a counterattack. Jiaotong University was caught off guard and was invaded into the hinterland. Suddenly, a kick hit the goal, but the kicker was already offside, so it was invalid even if it hit the goal.

Central University Loses Six Consecutive Goals 112

Jiaotong University used the short pass method to break through the Central University defense line. The right wing Xue Wenxiu picked the ball with precision, and the left wing Fei Fuxu shot with power. Central University's dragon gate lost the second goal. In the next twenty minutes, Jiaotong University continued to add five goals, which was extremely easy. Gong Yibin won the third goal and shot it while falling, which was very beautiful. Wan Mian's winning of the fourth goal was due to his own dexterity. The fifth goal was scored when Xue Wenxiu kicked a corner kick and fell into the crowd, and the Central University internal guard kicked it in himself. The sixth goal was scored by Fei Fuxu with a backhand kick, which was calm and powerful, thus winning the seventh goal. Liu Ximeng broke through and went straight in, and the goalkeeper got it back and lost it again. As a result, Jiaotong University won by a score of seven goals.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 114

— Hai Ke

A: You look troubled. Is something on your mind?

B: Yes. Did you see how hard it's raining? My wife went out without an umbrella.

A: Why worry about that? She'll just duck into some shop to avoid the rain.

B: That's exactly what I'm worried about. Once the rain stops, I fear she'll come back with a bunch of things and a shocking bill.

A: Mr. C is very extravagant. I don't know how he makes a living.

B: He relies entirely on other people's feet to maintain his livelihood.

A: So, does he own a shoe store?

B: No. He teaches people to dance.

Housewife (coming into the kitchen in the afternoon and seeing a pair of chopsticks, a wine cup, and two empty bowls with dregs on the table, angrily asks her maid): Humph! Has your lover been here again? You gave him our food and tea.

Maid (blushing): No, that's not it. Those two half-empty bowls are leftover food from lunch. I gave them to the big yellow dog next door.

Housewife: Who are you fooling? Does that big yellow dog use chopsticks and drink wine too?

Maid: I...I...I'm teaching him.

A: Your father is a very polite man. Whenever he sees me, he always stands up.

B: Yes, he often does the same when he sees my son.

Record of the Unveiling of the Monument to the Former Principal of the Minli School 115

— Ms. Ye Hua

Two years after the beginning of the new education in our country, that is, in the 30th year of the reign of Emperor Guangxu in the late Qing Dynasty, Minli Middle School emerged on the Huangxie River. The founder was Mr. Su Junshang, whom we praise today. At that time, the number of students who came to study was less than seventy, and the scale was simple. Compared with today's 1,548 students, 86 teachers, tens of thousands of alumni, and graduates all over the country, the school building is grander than a university, the difference is incalculable. Even if it is said that the current principal, Mr. Su Yingjie, has worked hard to achieve this, we should still remember that Mr. Junshang laid the foundation. The school held the unveiling ceremony of Mr. Junshang's monument at 10:30 a.m. on the 6th of this month. The reporter admired the man, so he attended with his family and recorded the grand occasion as follows.

The Monument The monument is located in the school's second sports field, in front of the new building built this year. The monument is rectangular in shape, with commemorative inscriptions in Chinese and English engraved on all sides. A steel half-body statue of Mr. Su is embedded on the top front, created by the artist Zhang Meisun, making people look up to it with admiration. At the top back is a steel pattern painted by Mr. Su's sixth son, Zuqi, which implies emphasis on commerce and learning, and hopes to promote it in the future. The idea is very beautiful and pleasing. It is said that railings will be added in the future to enhance the appearance. On that day, gifts from all walks of life were numerous, and wreaths surrounded the front and back of the monument, creating a solemn scene, which can be compared with Bismarck holding flowers to worship the old Emperor William.

Commemorative Words The Director of the Municipal Bureau of Education, Mr. Xu Tao, arrived early in the morning and left after attending for more than an hour. Ma Xiangbo arrived the latest. He is ninety-one years old and in high spirits. When he gave his speech, the whole field was silent. Ma said that people are like sheep, and the government is like a shepherd holding a whip. The sheep only listen to the shepherd's orders, and their likes and dislikes are determined by others. There is no freedom in the world, and nothing is more unequal than this. Only a country that is formed by gathering people can maintain its equality and independent dignity if its people are rich in equality and independence. Mr. Junshang was able to establish a school under a despotic regime to cultivate people's equality and independence. His contribution is great and his ambition is admirable. Finally, he encouraged the students of the school to take Junshang's spirit as their spirit and Junshang's morality as their morality. Then, the representatives of the alumni association, Zhou Shoujuan, and the student union, Hu Jixun, delivered speeches. The words were short and meaningful, and they were very moving.

Commemorative Text The inscription on the monument was written by Sun Yengeng of Wujiang. The text reads: Ten years after Mr. Su's death, the teachers and staff of Minli School and his children missed his merits and virtues. They sighed and said, "South of the Yangtze River and on the Huangpu River, among the businessmen and industrialists who founded schools, there are Chengzhong in the north, Pudong in the east, and Minli in the south. The Ye and Yang families all have auspicious metal and stone to commemorate them, but Mr. Su alone is missing. There is no way to respect his virtues and repay his merits." They told the student council and the alumni association about this. Everyone said, "It is appropriate to erect a monument," and asked me to write the inscription. I said, "I am an old friend of Mr. Su. I know the Su family the most. How can I refuse to write?" The Su family has four brothers. The eldest is Benli, the second is Benyan, the third is Benqiao, and the youngest is Benhao. Benyan is Mr. Su. Benqiao is the current principal, Mr. Yingjie. He wanted to save the country through education and spent money to build this school. In the 30th year of the reign of Emperor Guangxu in the late Qing Dynasty, Mr. Yingjie was in charge of teaching affairs, and Mr. Su was in charge of school affairs. The Su family's wealth cannot be compared with that of the Ye and Yang families, so it is conceivable how difficult it was to create this school. Mr. Su was a heroic man. He did not hesitate to spend even ten thousand gold if it was something he should do. Therefore, his wealth was only average, but in the fifteen years before and after, the school's expenses relied on Mr. Su's support for most of the amount, as recorded in the epitaph written by Yao. However, Mr. Su's position was that of general manager, which is now called manager. He was in charge of everything in the school, not just finance. Mr. Su was the leader of the business community and was famous all over the world. He used his spare time to manage the school, and he had a high vision. Therefore, all major matters such as land allocation, foundation laying, art house, school relocation, land purchase, expansion, and application for funds and subsidies, although Mr. Yingjie worked hard, could be carried out smoothly thanks to Mr. Su's efforts. After Mr. Su's death, school affairs were concentrated on Mr. Yingjie, and he realized how virtuous and hardworking he was. The virtue of the Ye and Yang families lies in their ability to spend a lot of money to serve the people of their hometowns, but they did not participate in anything else. Compared with Mr. Su, how were their efforts and leisure? It is appropriate that people still miss him after his death and seek to make him immortal. Therefore, they collected more than 900 yuan of silver and erected a monument between the east and west school buildings. The teaching staff contributed five-tenths, the alumni association two-tenths, and the student union three-tenths. It should be recorded according to the rules. Alas, it has been ten years since Mr. Su's death. When I walked around the school, I felt that every tile, every brick, every grass, and every tree had Mr. Su's spirit in it. Why? I hope that the teachers and staff will take Mr. Su's heart as their heart, work diligently, and establish the people's workshop. The alumni association and the student union should contribute to construction and promote Mr. Su's glory. When they are on the road, passers-by will be surprised by their uniqueness, just like the people of the Song Dynasty said of Hu An's disciples, "This is a student of the Su family." Then Mr. Su's spirit will always be poured into the hearts and kidneys of everyone. Is this not more than erecting a monument to compare with Ye and Yang? This is what I and all of you should strive for together.

Anecdotes of Mr. Qiu Chuyu 116

— Dui Tian

Mr. Qiu, named Yanxi, with the courtesy name Chuyu, was from Liaoli, Dongshan, Wuxian, Jiangsu. His ancestors were farmers. When Mr. Qiu began to study, he dropped out of school halfway due to poverty and then entered the Kedahong firm to work. However, Mr. Qiu's ambition to improve himself never wavered. In his spare time, he often read books and newspapers to encourage himself. At that time, members of the Tongmenghui published newspapers such as "Min Hu," "Min Xu," "Min Li," and "Min Quan," which advocated revolution. Mr. Qiu was impressed by them. Every time a new issue came out, he would buy and save it from the first issue to the last. At this time, the Qing government was vigorously arresting party members. Not only were the writers in danger of being killed, but the readers were also in danger and dared not buy and read them openly. Only Mr. Qiu resolutely bought and read them as usual and saved them as usual. Others ridiculed him. The "Min Hu," "Min Xu," and other newspapers were published and suspended from time to time, and now they are lost without a trace. Only those saved by Mr. Qiu are complete from beginning to end. Now that the revolution has been accomplished, and the National Government has proposed collecting revolutionary history, Mr. Qiu planned to send the entire collection to the Revolutionary History Museum. Unfortunately, he died of scarlet fever in the winter of the previous year, which was a pity for those who heard about it. His wife, Ms. Song, gave birth to a daughter. The son of Mr. Qiu's third elder brother was adopted as his heir. After his death, his affairs were bleak. Mr. Qiu's friends sent the entire collection of "Min Hu," "Min Xu," "Min Quan," and "Min Li" newspapers saved by Mr. Qiu during his lifetime to the National Government to help with the revolutionary history in the future. It is said that a certain important person said that this kind of revolutionary historical material is extremely precious because it is not easy to collect. Therefore, the National Government plans to give a considerable reward to show its commemoration.

An Interview with Ms. Hu Die 117

— Mian Zi

The social lives, love lives, or family lives of some movie stars often receive great attention from many newspapers and magazines. Especially in the United States, even a female star losing a flower on her lapel becomes a good source of information for many movie newspapers and magazines. Recently, the case of Ms. Hu Die and Mr. Lin Xuehuai breaking off their engagement in the Chinese film industry has naturally attracted much attention from society. Therefore, I personally visited Ms. Hu at the Mingxing Company yesterday and had the following conversation with her.

Ms. Hu said, "I have always been opposed to the romantic atmosphere in the film industry in the past. For many years, I have been engaged in the film industry and I am fortunate to be able to maintain a good reputation. I am also fortunate to have won the sincere sympathy of many people in society. This matter is indeed unexpected. Although the outside world has some doubts about me, my pure heart will still be revealed clearly in the future. I don't want to say any more nonsense about this matter now. My life from now on will be to work harder in the film industry. I often believe that the success of a career is the best guarantee for all credit and reputation." Speaking of this, Ms. Hu remained silent for a long time, then said, "Sir, please go and see my new film, "The Singing Girl Red Peony". Women always have to suffer some losses." Ms. Hu suddenly smiled.

Later, I met the director of the company, Mr. Zheng Zhiqi. Mr. Zheng said, "Ms. Hu is very hardworking in film. This incident is really unfortunate for her. She has made many films in Mingxing. The most outstanding one is "Broken Qin Building". She is now working on the production of "The Tale of Laughter and Tears", and the results are getting better and better. As for "The Singing Girl Red Peony", it is also a sound film starring her. I believe it will have good results after it is released in the future. In the past few days, she has not been negative because of this unfortunate incident. According to her, it is inevitable for a person to have unexpected things in their life, so she still goes to the company to shoot films every day without any slack. I think, with Ms. Hu's current status, if she is willing to work hard, she will definitely have a lot of hope in the future."

Travels in Southeast Asia (96) 118

— Ling Hua

Wang Yantao said, "Since I came to Burma, I have also been infected by its customs. I seek a view of life where freedom is the best policy. I regard wealth as very light. But if the Burmese did not communicate with the outside world in the past and were purely Burmese, it would be fine. Everyone is free and good at giving to help each other. Now, the British, Indians, Chinese, and Japanese, all those who come to Burma, use all kinds of wisdom to seize the sources of wealth and leave. But those who come are not willing to give, so the Burmese are impoverished." I have heard that the Mongols are also like this, and they regard property as very light. This is because they have been influenced by Buddhism. I don't understand why the rich in China also know Buddhism, but they are very stingy. Why? Master Wanhui praised the high level of education and morality of the Burmese, and regarded the Chinese as vulgar, stingy, greedy, and scrambling for rights, making themselves beasts of burden for their children and grandchildren. Their style of chivalry and integrity is far from that of the Burmese. I said, "It's a pity that we don't use Buddhism to move the Europeans." My friend Zhang Xiangwen, a geographer, once said to me, "Try to observe the Mongols' heroism, which once overthrew the world. But since they were influenced by Buddhism, they have been docile to this day. If you want Europeans to be docile, you must spread Buddhism widely." I don't understand why those who study Buddhism in China do not have a single thing to repay their kindness or promote the Dharma, but only seek blessings and longevity, which are inferior blessings. Alas, there is a custom in Burma. Before the rainy season comes, around March and April of the lunar calendar, there is a custom of splashing water. Men and women splash water on each other. After the water-splashing ceremony, they can fall in love freely. Unmarried people can get married freely, and married people can freely change their spouses. But the water splashed is fragrant water and clear water, and bad water cannot be used. Parents cannot interfere, and masters have no right to interfere. The length of this festival is about one week. The biggest splashing is for three days. But even if it is not the water-splashing festival, men and women can divorce freely at any time. However, the biggest change of the year is during the water-splashing festival. According to this, it is the same custom as the Zhou Li's Mid-Spring February Situ, the media officer in charge of gathering unmarried men and women, and the runners are not prohibited. The fourth month of the solar calendar is the second month of our lunar calendar. But I read in the newspaper that Annam (not sure) also has this custom. Because of the water-splashing, there was a big disturbance. During the festival, the streets are full of water-splashing, and people are splashed when they meet, to the point of disturbing order and causing injuries. It is said that the meaning of water-splashing is that because the rainy season is coming, it is a hot season, and everyone must take a shower. They teach each other and it becomes a custom of respect and love.

Warmth in My Heart (333) 119

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Green Skirts Visit the Teacher Asking for Characters Diligently; Talented Women Feast in Brothels Speaking Generously of Military Affairs

Luyi's room occupies a quarter of a three-story house, in a厢房 (xiāngfáng, side room) on the east side of the upstairs, plus a large pavilion room in the back. The arrangement of the furniture seems to have changed a bit. The usual way is to turn the xiāngfáng upstairs into a study, and the large pavilion room in the back into a bedroom. In fact, what is called a study is just a study in a brothel. It is called a study, but there is not a single book. Needless to say. The furniture is all rented from furniture shops. There are many furniture shops in Shanghai that rely on brothels for their livelihood. For example, a whole room of redwood furniture costs a certain amount of money to rent per period. There is one bed, several tables, several chairs, etc., forming a set. This set is called a room. When it is time to move at the end of each period, it is moved from this alley to that alley, or from that room to that room. If that kind of furniture became knowledgeable, it would have seen a lot of stupidity in the world with its cold eyes. If it could open its mouth, it could tell all the foolishness of the world. The so-called decoration of a study in a brothel is also the same set from the furniture shop. A redwood kang bed is placed in the center. Although there is also a kang table, it is removed to provide for the needs of guests smoking opium. In addition, there is a redwood eight-immortal table, and a row of armchairs and tea tables along the wall. There is also a desk with drawers. However, when you pull open the drawers of the desk, what is placed inside is the paper ingots and yuanbin burned by the prostitutes at the end of each month. They are folded in stacks there. There are also the rough shoe soles made by the old maids, along with scissors, needles, and thimbles. If you dig further down, there are empty cigarette tins and broken light bulbs. Luyi's newly furnished room naturally has a bit of a new atmosphere. Although all the furniture in the room is rented, she wants to choose the best. At that time, foreign-style furniture was not very popular in Beili (brothels). They thought that Western-style furniture was too expensive. Those spring sofas and chairs are good when they are new. But in less than a period, the place where you sit becomes a pool, and it has long lost its elasticity. There are some skinny friends whose bones have already protruded from their skin. When they sit on that kind of chair with spring circles protruding on the outside, the two bony things collide, which is obviously uncomfortable. It is better to have the kind of Yang Guifei couch that is unique to China. There are also many drawers in foreign tables, but the boards inside often fall off. If you put something in the first drawer, you may find it in the last drawer. Especially the paint on foreign furniture is as delicate as a beauty's skin. If you put something hot on it, it will leave a mark. You have to use eau de toilette to wipe it often. It is a bit unwilling to have people use the effort of serving a young lady to serve foreign furniture.

Reasons for the Recent Drastic Changes in the Auxiliary Coin Market Price 124

In recent ten days of this month, drastic changes have occurred in the general exchange market. 角洋 (smaller silver coins) have gradually reduced to within 11 jiao, and copper coins are only around 260 coins. The reason is nothing more than the extreme shortage of physical coins. This has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Now we have learned that there are still situations in the mix. Since Guangjiao (Guangdong 角 coins) were purchased and shipped by the Dalian gang in August and September, there was a period of exhaustion and panic. Later, due to the limited social demand, it was not of great importance. Now that the end of the year is approaching and the need for the coins has increased, while the supply is insufficient, they are competing to raise prices, resulting in the current special phenomenon. In the recent few days, the upward trend has been particularly strong, which has attracted the attention of neighboring ports. In the past two days, they have prepared cash and shipped it to Shanghai to relieve the urgent needs of the Shanghai market. The number is more than hundreds of thousands, purely gathered from Zhenjiang, Yangzhou, and the Yangtze River area. Finally, yesterday's market price plummeted. As for the inside story of the continuous and rapid decline of copper coins, it was caused by the purchase and shipment from Hong Kong and Guangdong. It is also heard that Japan is purchasing purple copper raw materials, and some profit-seekers are even daring to melt old copper coins (with dragon patterns) into copper cakes to meet the demand, resulting in an extreme shortage of cash in the market. Currently, this leak has not stopped, and it is feared that the market price of copper coins will inevitably continue to decline.

Recent Wheat Soars by One Qian 131

What is even more important is that due to the National Lunar New Year, the standard for this month is up to the day of Nianri. Today is the anniversary of the Communist Party's uprising in Guangzhou. The French Concession authorities received a confidential report early on that a large number of reactionary elements plan to divide into four groups and gather at 7:00 AM in Caojiadu Yinghua Li, Pudong Yangshupu, Dapu Bridge in the French Concession, and the Minguo Road area in the Chinese-controlled territory, to demonstrate in Nanjing Road. Commander Xiong's Injuries Improved Yesterday 136

Follow-up Report on the Shanghai-Hankou Plane Crash

Four Bodies Examined and Separately Buried

Shanghai-Hankou Aviation Still Operating as Usual

China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai No. 2 aircraft, scheduled to fly to Nanjing, Jiujiang, and Hankou at 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, crashed into the large mast of a sand barge near the dock ten minutes after takeoff. The plane's left wing (mistakenly written as the right wing yesterday) broke, the mast snapped, and the fuselage overturned on the shore. As a result, American pilot Bell, mechanical assistant Bian Fugen, passenger Yin Wenlong, and Russian woman Mrs. Anderfei, a total of four people, died. Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui, General Headquarters Advisor Yang Yongtai, and Xiong's trusted bodyguard Zeng Chunfan were seriously injured. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, various news obtained yesterday are summarized as follows:

Jiang and Song's Telegrams: After the accident the day before yesterday, the Garrison Headquarters sent an urgent telegram to Chairman Jiang of the National Government in Nanchang. A reply telegram was soon received expressing deep concern and instructing careful treatment. The Garrison Headquarters telegraphed Jiang again the night before yesterday, describing the medical treatment process. Yesterday morning, a telegram was received from Chairman Jiang, stating, "It is very gratifying that the injuries have been reduced." He also requested that the condition be reported twice, day and night. The Garrison Headquarters has complied with the order. In addition, Finance Minister Song Ziwen is also very concerned about this matter. At 9:00 AM yesterday, he telegraphed Dr. Niu Huisheng, inquiring in detail about the current state of Xiong's treatment. Dr. Niu immediately telegraphed back the facts.

Xiong's Injury Reduced: At 10:00 AM yesterday, Doctors Niu Huisheng and Hui Lin went to the Orthopedic Hospital to examine the injuries of Xiong Shihui and Zeng Chunfan. Shortly after, Dr. Berto, Director of Baolong Hospital on Baker Road and head of surgery, along with German doctor Gu Yuqi, also came to examine them. At that time, Xiong was in good spirits. There was no pain in the bone fracture site, and there were no signs of inflammation. His speech was very clear. His complexion was greenish-gray the day before yesterday, but it had turned grayish-white yesterday. After further diagnosis and treatment by Dr. Niu and others in the afternoon, there was even more improvement. According to Dr. Niu Huisheng, Xiong's condition was indeed reduced compared to the day before yesterday. If there are no special changes in the coming days, his life is definitely out of danger. According to the director of Baolong Hospital, Xiong is gradually getting out of the danger zone.

Announcing the Condition: Yesterday, the Orthopedic Hospital announced the condition of Xiong Shihui and Zeng Chunfan. The transcript is as follows: (1) First report on Commander Xiong's condition: Dr. Niu Huilin came to the hospital for examination at 6:00 PM on the 9th. The situation was still good, but there was a lack of urination. At 6:45, Niu Huisheng diagnosed and treated him, using a rubber tube to release it, and then got urine. The chemical test showed slight internal injuries. He slept soundly for four hours at night. On the morning of the 10th, his complexion was better, the temperature was 99.2, the pulse was 28, and the breathing was 23, so a detailed examination of the whole body was made. Because the urine was less than usual, Dr. Cao Chentao, an expert in reproductive and urinary medicine, was specially invited to treat the kidney. Dr. Cao was formerly at Peking Union Medical College. Pulmonary expert Dr. Kuang Cuie, director of the pediatric hospital's pulmonary department, was also invited to check the lungs. Then Dr. Niu Huisheng and Doctors Zeng Baohan and Chen Jiayu carefully examined the wound, and the bone fracture site was examined with X-rays. The phenomenon was still good after surgery. The airline also invited British doctor O'Hara to visit the hospital. Liquid diet, (2) Second report at 3:30 PM yesterday, Commander Xiong was in good spirits from 10:00 AM to 4:00 PM, both when awake and asleep. There was no pain in the injured area. Dr. Kuang Cuie, a specialist in lung examination, was specially invited to check the lungs in the morning, and there was no internal injury. The temperature was 99.6 in the afternoon, the pulse was 108, the breathing was 20, and the symptoms were reduced compared to the previous day.

Zeng's Condition Worsens: Yesterday, the condition of Xiong's bodyguard Zeng Chunfan worsened. The hospital's announcement is recorded as follows: (1) First report at 10:00 AM yesterday, on the evening of the 9th, the temperature was 101.2, the pulse was 130, the breathing was 33, and there was no urine. Dean Niu Huisheng used a rubber tube to release urine. After the chemical test, there was no internal injury to the kidneys. The broken right humerus was already connected and was not painful. He slept for more than three hours last night, breathing fast, because of the concussion to the brain, he was not very clear-headed. On the morning of the 10th, urine had been discharged by himself. Doctors Zeng Baohan and Chen Jiayu changed the dressing on the wound. At 10:30, Dean Niu also went to examine it. There was not much change in the wound, and the fever was slightly lower, 98.6. Because of the rapid breathing, Dr. Kuang Cuie was also invited to examine the lungs. (2) Second report at 4:00 PM yesterday, he was sleepy from 10:00 AM to 4:00 PM, mentally exhausted, and there was no change in the injured area. There was pain in the chest when breathing. The temperature was 99.6 in the afternoon, the pulse was 124, and the breathing was 29. The symptoms are still in a dangerous period.

Condolences Arrive: Yesterday, those who went to the Orthopedic Hospital to express their condolences included Zhang Qun, Huang Boqiao, Duan Honggang, Li Zhaohuan, Hu Hongji, Xu Fu, Zhu Peide, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Xunyong, Jiang Baiqi, Yang Shuzhuang, Tang Naikang, Cao Haosen, Du Yuesheng, Yang Xiaotian, Xu Shiying, Yan Shenyu, and all the executive and supervisory members of the Municipal Party Department. On the foreign side, Deputy Consul Tanaka represented Japanese representative Shigemitsu Aoi, and Consul General Murai went to express their condolences, all of whom were thanked by Jiang Yi, director of the adjutant office of the Command Headquarters. Yang's Condition Unchanged: Advisor Yang Yongtai of the General Headquarters, his injury showed no change yesterday. The reporter of this newspaper went to Baolong Hospital yesterday to investigate. According to Yang's attendants, Yang was able to sleep peacefully, but the back pain did not stop. In the morning, Dr. Berto, the director of the hospital, came to examine him personally. X-rays had not been taken yet. He said that there was no worry about life. Yang was able to eat milk porridge, but his limbs were sore, and his spirit was not as good as before. The cough was also more severe, and there was still blood in the sputum. The doctor said that it was caused by a concussion to the lungs, and it was okay.

Examination of the Bodies: Four male and female corpses, including Yin Wenlong, Bian Fugen, American pilot Bell, and Russian woman Mrs. Anderfei, were carried into the Forensic Examination Office on Fielun Road by the police. Except for Bell, who was of American nationality and should be reported to the U.S. Assessor's Office in Shanghai to send an inspector to examine and order the burial, although Mrs. Anderfei in the remaining three corpses was of Russian nationality, Russia has abolished consular jurisdiction, so she should be examined by our country's judicial organs together with the corpses of Yin and Bian. Yesterday morning, the Special District Local Court immediately sent Prosecutor Guo Huaipu, along with a forensic doctor and a clerk, to the office upon receiving the report. First, forensic doctor Wei examined Bian Fugen's body according to law. Then Bian Rengen, the deceased's younger brother, filed a case, claiming that the deceased was his biological brother and was only twenty-three years old. He was not at the scene when the plane crashed, and only heard the bad news in the evening. He requested to be exempted from autopsy. Prosecutor Guo approved the request, ordered Bian Rengen to sign a guarantee, and took the body for burial. Then the Russian woman's body was examined, but her family members were not in Shanghai. A friend of the same nationality, Mo Yingji, came to the case and requested to take the body. According to him, the deceased opened a tailoring shop in Hankou and came to Shanghai a few days ago for business affairs. She took the plane back to Hankou yesterday, which led to the disaster. Prosecutor Guo also instructed Mo Yingji to sign a guarantee and coffin the body. Finally, Yin Wenlong's remains were examined, and Yin Wenlin, the elder brother of the corpse, came to the case and requested. The judge approved the request to have him sign the guarantee and take the body away.

Pilot's Funeral: After the crash of China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai No. 2 aircraft, the tragic death of pilot Bell will be held at the American Funeral Home at 3:00 PM today. Then the President McKinley will transport the remains back to Fort Wayne, Indiana, in the United States for burial. It is also heard that he will be buried in front of the Lafayette General's memorial tombstone. It is heard that most of the veterans of the European War in this city will go to the funeral at that time, because Bell is also one of the veteran aviators. According to Bell, he was thirty-six years old and served in the United States Aviation Service during the European War, and he had a great reputation at that time. Bell joined the Lafayette Air Force in February 1917 and shot down nine German aircraft, making him one of the four outstanding talents of the team and an indispensable talent in the American aviation industry. On May 22, 1918, Bell was shot and wounded and captured by the Germans. He was not freed until the end of the Great War. The U.S. government awarded Bell a first-class medal in view of his great achievements, and the French government also awarded him a medal. The Lafayette Air Force's record mentions Bell's life a lot. The following is an excerpt: "Bell was captured by the Germans, and our team suffered a great loss. Bell's perseverance and spirit are beyond the reach of ordinary people. He went deep into the enemy's territory to scout the enemy's situation, and he never retreated despite the dangers. His driving skills, concealment, tolerance, and hard work are admirable and give our army great benefits." After the Great War, Bell joined commercial aviation and served as a driver for Ford Airlines, a technician inspector for the Aviation Department of the U.S. Department of Commerce, and a chief of operations for Chicago General Aviation. He then joined China National Aviation Corporation as a pilot. Bell had a flying record of 3,500 hours during his lifetime.

Preferential Compensation: As for Yin Wenlong's corpse, it was temporarily buried at the Universal Funeral Home yesterday. His Shanghai residence has only one grandmother. After Yin's mother and wife arrive from Hankou, the funeral will be officially held. The body of the mechanical assistant Bian Fugen was also buried yesterday. His parents and wife in Wuxi have all arrived in Shanghai. The airline will fully bear the funeral expenses of Bian and the American pilot. According to Nie Kaiyi, the airline plans to give special preferential treatment in the future. The amount can be determined after the board of directors approves it.

Cause of the Accident: According to the Great American Evening News, according to Chen, the mechanical assistant of China National Aviation Corporation, the reason for the plane crash was actually due to the flight being too low, the turning was too fast, and the weight carried was relatively heavy. Chen also said that the reason why the pilot of the Shanghai No. 2 aircraft in distress could not fly high was because the mail loaded was quite heavy, and there were five passengers in addition. After the plane collided with the mast, the left wing of the plane broke and the fuselage lost its balance, causing a major disaster. Report to Wang: The reporter of this newspaper interviewed Nie Kaiyi and important officials of the company yesterday. According to them, the company sent officials to Beijing the night before yesterday to meet with Chairman Wang Boqun and report the details in detail. In short, this matter was a sudden event, and both parties were extremely unfortunate, and it was even more unfortunate for the fledgling Chinese aviation industry. From now on, the company will be more cautious and hopes for public support so that the aviation industry will become more developed. Regular Flights: At 8:00 AM yesterday, the Shanghai-Hankou route of China National Aviation Corporation was still operating as usual. The plane was Hankou No. 4, driven by American pilot Costed. The passengers on board in Shanghai were Mrs. Gao Jianlong (Chinese), Count Ciano, the Italian Consul General in Shanghai, and Mai Duoli, the Italian Commercial Attaché. Arresting the crew is an unreasonable act in the world. According to common practice, if the main mast is broken by a plane crash, the airline should be asked for compensation." News This Morning: At about 1:00 AM this morning, Dr. Niu went to the Orthopedic Hospital again for examination.
