Business Representatives Persuaded Minister Kong Yesterday 138

National Government Orders Retention

After Kong Xiangxi, the newly appointed Minister of Industry, was clearly appointed by the National Government, he firmly requested to resign and came to Shanghai last week to rest. The news obtained yesterday is recorded as follows:

Talks of Resignation: Because the National News Agency has reported Kong's resignation news for several days, the reporter drove to Kong's residence on West Ames Road yesterday for an interview. Mr. Kong was out, and a secretary received him and answered the following: (Reporter asked) Minister Kong is in charge of industry and commerce, and public opinion is enthusiastic. This time, he was reappointed as Minister of Industry. The business community is deeply grateful. Why did he suddenly become passive? (Answer) Kong's reasons for resigning have been detailed in the letter of resignation, and you have already read it. Now I will tell you what I know. Kong has been running around for national affairs for many years and has been exhausted. He has always had a strong sense of responsibility and is courageous in doing things. He must carefully examine the affairs of the department, no matter how big or small. As a result, he suffered from overwork and illness. He was admitted to the hospital for treatment in the summer of this year for more than two months, but he has not recovered. The doctor strongly urged him to take a few months of rest in order to fully recover and avoid recurrence. The military affairs have just been settled, and all political affairs are urgently waiting for proper planning and aftermath. The Fourth Plenary Session is of great importance, and he has to attend with illness in order to make a contribution. Now that the unification has just been completed, and the central government is trying to refresh its political power, the central government is recruiting talents from all parties to seek governance with great enthusiasm. Therefore, the resignation letter stated that the section of avoiding position and giving way to the virtuous is sincere. (Question) Shanxi fellow villagers in various places have repeatedly telegraphed the National Government to appoint Kong as the chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government. Kong is an advanced revolutionary in Shanxi Province. At this time when Shanxi is dilapidated, does he also intend to return to Shanxi to preside over provincial affairs? (Answer) Shanxi has been under the rule of Yan Xishan for nineteen years. It is heard that the forces in the province are divided into north and south factions. Kong is a central figure with a kind personality and a strict attitude. He has done his best to create social undertakings and has achieved remarkable results. He has always been impartial to all factions and has a happy relationship with all of them. The factions and local people are very fond of Kong. Therefore, after Yan left Shanxi, the people of Shanxi sent letters and telegrams and sent representatives to urge him to return to Shanxi to preside over the provincial situation. Zhao Daiwen and others also telegraphed Kong to ask him to return to Shanxi and maintain the Shanxi situation to the end in order to save his hometown and stabilize the northwest. However, Kong believes that his body has not recovered and still needs to be rested, and Shanxi has just been destroyed. The position of chairman of the provincial government cannot be done by anyone who is talented, both civil and military, and has extraordinary energy. The position of Minister of Industry has been repeatedly resigned, and he is willing to assist the government in the capacity of a Central Committee member in the construction of everything. Therefore, he has politely declined and firmly rejected the good intentions of all parties. At this point, the reporter resigned and left.

National Government Retention Order: After receiving Kong's resignation letter, the National Government immediately ordered to retain him, which is recorded below: The government chooses people for the Ministry of Industry, because the minister has a great body and a keen mind, and he is familiar with the matter, so he is proposed for this position. The times are difficult, so it is difficult to make it difficult for him to seek great salvation. The request to withdraw the order should not be discussed. It should be notified immediately and reported to the Executive Yuan for notification. This order.

Business Community's Retention: After the various commercial organizations in this city heard that Kong had resigned as Minister of Industry, they telegraphed the National Government and the administrative authorities to retain Kong. Yesterday, business leaders in this city, Yu Qiaqing, Wen Lanting, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, and Director of the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau Zhao Jinqing, etc., went to Kong's residence together to meet Minister Kong and asked him to consider the difficulties of the business community, follow the public opinion, and take office immediately. Kong replied to Yu and others, saying, "I am really unable to do it due to lack of energy. At this time, the central government is recruiting talents from all parties and is eagerly seeking governance. It is sincere to give way to the virtuous. Thank you for your visit." National Goods Association Urgently Telephoned: Respectfully salute Minister Kong, Ministry of Industry, Nanjing, the two ministries of industry, commerce, agriculture, and mines are merged into the Ministry of Industry, and Your Excellency is specially appointed as Minister, which is very happy. I was planning to send a respectful telegram to congratulate you, but suddenly I heard that you expressed negativity and have submitted a letter to the National Government to request that the order be withdrawn, which is very disturbing. I think that since you have been in charge of industrial and commercial administration, you have spared no effort in promoting national goods. This time, you are again the head of the industry, and I deeply hope that you will be familiar with the matter and expand your grand plan. In addition to directly telephoning the National Government to request retention, I will send a telegram to express my feelings. Please dismiss your intention to resign and take office immediately, and implement the Premier's plan to save the country through industry to maintain the people's livelihood, Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation.

Silk Factory Industry's Method of Allocating Debt 143

Will Be Submitted for Approval and Implementation

The silk factory industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai was on the verge of bankruptcy due to sluggish sales and losses. It was publicly agreed to submit a request to the government to issue 10 million yuan of silk industry public bonds in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai to provide relief. It has been approved by Chairman Jiang and Finance Minister Song, etc., and is being handled by Vice Minister of Finance Zhang. Later, it was feared that there would be malpractices in the proposed method of allocation and amortization, and the representatives selected by the silk factory industry were ordered to carefully review the matter. Representatives from silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai held a meeting on the 3rd of this month. Under the collective discussion, the meeting was still fruitless because of concerns that the proposed method was inappropriate. Later, the representatives decided to recommend Wang Xiaolai to visit Vice Minister Zhang and request that the department instruct a proper method to be followed. It is now known that the government has agreed to issue the silk industry relief public bonds, because white silk is related to international trade and should be rescued. However, the problem of allocation and amortization, in addition to amortizing the debt principal, is still based on the previous agreement that 20 taels of silver will be withdrawn for each silk load at the time of export, and the deadline and other items are based on the outline of the previous agreement. The level of distribution of debt is very problematic, and the representatives have repeatedly discussed it meticulously, but there is a lack of a proper method. Generally, according to the number of vehicles, it is necessary to wait for each factory to throw out a package of seasonal silk and receive a public bond of 200 yuan, and so on, in order to prevent abuses and confusions. The opinions and revised distribution methods are now being prepared and submitted to Vice Minister of Finance Zhang for approval and implementation. Judging from this, the issuance of silk industry relief public bonds will not be far away.

Difficulties in Yangtse River Navigation 149

Shallow Waters...Numerous Bandits

"YiBao" Runs Aground and Escapes Danger: The "Yibin" of the Jiejiang Company, returning to Shanghai from the upper reaches, departed from Yichang. Due to the sharp decline in river water levels, it ran aground downstream of Yichang. It was first stranded due to shallow water, and then some screws fell off the machinery. After sailing out of the shallows, it encountered two more groundings. The ship telegraphed Yichang for assistance and a vessel was dispatched to the accident site to pull it out of the dangerous shoal. Meanwhile, the loose screws were repaired, and it set sail for Shanghai. The ship will be inspected in Shanghai before resuming service.

"Yu Shun" Already Freed From Shoal: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Yu Shun" ran aground on the Yangtze River in Hankou, as reported yesterday. It is now learned that yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, after several lighters cleared the cargo from each hold, reducing the draft, the ship floated. Then, a small tugboat towed it. The Shanghai office received a telegram from Hankou yesterday afternoon, stating that the "Yu Shun" had been pulled out of the shallows. Whether there is damage still needs to be inspected.

No Warning Signs on the Upper Yangtze: On the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the rise and fall of sandbars vary, making navigation very difficult. Traditionally, customs officials in each area would send river patrol officers to measure and verify the river conditions at any time and then announce any changes to hidden reefs and sandbars, either by posting notices, placing red lights, or setting up warning markers, so that ships sailing up and down the river could avoid them. Since the Yuezhou customs officials were kidnapped by bandits while surveying the river this year, no one has dared to go to measure and verify the changes in reefs and shoals from Xindi to Jianli and Shishou, upstream of Hankou. As there have been no warning markers for a long time, since the water level dropped in winter, in just over a week, five or six ships have run aground and encountered bandits due to ignorance of the shoals and reefs.

Two Ships Encounter Bandits on the Yangtze: The Nissin Kisen Kaisha's Yangtze River steamer "Soyang Maru" was sailing downstream from Hankou to Shanghai. While passing between Qizhou and Huangzhou downstream, it was already night. Suddenly, gunfire erupted from the riverbank. The captain, knowing that bandits were planning to attack, immediately ordered full speed ahead and turned off the lights to sail in the dark to avoid being targeted by the bandits. After ten minutes, the bandits were unable to catch up, and they managed to escape. At the same time, the Taikoo's "Ta Tung", following behind downstream, also encountered bandits firing guns at Qizhou. The British soldiers stationed on the "Ta Tung" fired hundreds of rounds from machine guns, and the bandits fled. The passengers on both ships suffered a scare, but fortunately, there were no injuries.

Kidnapped Crew Members Released: Above Xindi, there are the most bandits along the river, specializing in robbing ships, often taking the crew away. After the special tax vessel "Xin Yunnan," which was stranded at Diaoguan, was robbed, the crew and sailors were all kidnapped. Also, two cooks from the Sanbei Dexing, after running aground downstream of Xindi, went ashore to shop and were also kidnapped by bandits. It was heard yesterday that the kidnapped people have all been released. According to those who escaped from the bandits' den, after the bandits kidnap the crew members, they must interrogate the sailors one by one, asking about the shipowner, how the chief mate is, and how they treat the workers. If the sailors say that the shipowner treats people harshly, the bandits will behead the shipowner, the chief mate, etc., and discard their bodies in the river. This has already happened once. According to what the sailors said, all the crew members who were kidnapped were killed. Those who went to the bandits' den, because most of them were from the lower reaches of the river, the bandit leaders did not force them to stay (as for those from the upper reaches who were kidnapped, they had to be forced to join the bandits). Each person was given two yuan for travel expenses and a piece of personal identification to be released to the riverside. The bandits would find a wooden raft going downstream to Hankou on their behalf. There were many checkpoints along the way. Showing the identification card would allow them to pass. People who came out of the bandits' den, along the way, there were restaurants, etc. If the bandits went to eat, they did not have to pay. It was practicing communism. If it was not communism and the released people went to eat, each meal cost 200 cash, regardless of how much they ate. Some people stayed in the bandit den for more than ten days, and some stayed for one or two days.

The Xinfeng Case is Transferred to Tianjin for Negotiation 151

In the case of the Japanese ship "Kageyama Maru" colliding with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Xinfeng", the responsibility is clear, and all losses should be compensated by the Japanese ship. However, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent a bill for compensation, but the Nippon Yusen Kaisha replied attempting to deny responsibility, only expressing regret and refusing to admit liability. Because the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company had obtained the Japanese shipowner's acknowledgment of responsibility and signed evidence, how could they be allowed to quibble? The pilot of the "Xinfeng" at the time of the collision, Bai Lin (who was also the owner of the "Xinfeng" ten years ago), is a strong witness in this case. The Japanese's cunning is not only contrary to justice but also harms the pilot's duty and reputation. Unless the Japanese ship compensates, fairness cannot be shown. The pilot also put forward reasons in his capacity as a witness and pilot, negotiating with Nippon Yusen Kaisha and demanding that they bear the responsibility for the collision. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's shipping department has now transferred the case to Tianjin because there is no branch of Nippon Yusen Kaisha in Shanghai, instructing the Tianjin office to negotiate nearby. According to reliable information received yesterday, the Japanese also know that they are at fault and are willing to reasonably compensate for the damaged parts of "Xinfeng", but the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company must order them to recognize and pay the full amount, so the struggle is still ongoing.

The Tobacco and Exchange Industry Proposes to Abolish Tobacco and Alcohol Licenses and Monopoly 155

Many tobacco and exchange shops in the Chinese districts sell tobacco, alcohol, and groceries. Considering the heavy taxation and harassment of tobacco and alcohol, a special meeting was convened to make a resolution. Opinions were drafted and submitted to the Executive Committee, and the association of soy sauce and liquor companies was solicited to jointly petition for the abolition, as recorded below: (1) A letter to the Executive Committee of the Tobacco and Exchange Industry Association states: "Dear Sirs, recently reading the newspaper, we learned that the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang has resolved to implement the abolition of customs duties and the reorganization of business taxes on January 1, 1931, reducing the burden on merchants. This is a good law and a beautiful intention, and we deeply appreciate it. However, with the establishment of new taxes, the existing similar ones should naturally be eliminated, so as not to burden our merchants again. The two items that are similar to business tax are the tobacco and alcohol monopoly and the tobacco and alcohol licenses. We hereby describe the situation of heavy taxation and harassment in detail below, and we hope that you will consider it. It is found that the taxes have already been paid separately at the place of origin for the merchant who transport the drought tobacco and the earth yellow shao wine, etc. Each time the merchant transport it to the store and sell it, they must pay the monopoly tax, otherwise they will be punished at a multiple of the price. This is a clear proof of the heavy tax, the merchants have been suffering a lot, they dare to be angry but dare not to speak out. The name of the monopoly has the meaning of the business and as to the license, the disturbance is even more serious, (A) when merchants set up a new store, there is no fee for the license to be obtained but the said office must charge an additional $1.20 in the name of handling the registration fee. The Baoshan sub-collection office is even more serious, when the merchants engages in both tobacco and alcohol, $1.20 will be added to each license to be applied. (B) Overdue fees are charged (i.e. expediting fee), the chapter states that the overdue fee for tobacco category A is 8 corners, the overdue fee for tobacco category B is 6 corners, the overdue fee for tobacco category C is 4 corners, and the overdue fee for tobacco category D is 2 corners. The situation for the alcohol category is the same, the tax will be charged additionally from the date of expiry (i.e. the 11th day of the 1st, 4th, 7th, and 10th months) to the date of termination (i.e. the end of the 3rd, 6th, 9th, and 12th months), in addition to the payment of the main items, to show a warning. The 4 words (added by month) were added to the said office by themselves, it is permissible to collect an additional 10% of the fee in the first month of each period, an additional 20% in the second month, and an additional 30% in the last month, the said fee are purely pocketed by the contractors. As mentioned above, in the event that big merchants are aware of the tax law, the said office will be flexible to exempt the fee, but for the small merchants who are not knowledge, they will be threatened to not to give up until they achieve their purpose of greed. Under the accumulation of prestige, there is no one to complain, in addition, the staff collects tips in private outside, not to let the people apply for the permit, and the act of favoritism covers up the resistance to the permit etc. Resulting in good merchants being filled with market prices in chaos, the legitimate business of the big merchants are suffering from its difficulties, and with reference to the receipts filled out by the said office to the tobacco and liquor merchants for the license in the past, it is stated (subject to investigation of the business is consistent with the amount of tax, the permit is allowed to be exchanged), which has certainly proved that the license tax is a business tax. Therefore, the reorganization of the business tax will give the former two taxes a cut, so as to achieve real benefits and avoid harsh burdens. Within our knowledge, we will jointly Chen the letter to your association, hoping that this opinion will be sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for approval. It is the fortune of the entire tobacco and alcohol industry. "The Association of Soy Sauce and Liquor Companies states: "Dear Sirs, in light of the news that the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang has resolved to implement the abolition of customs duties and the reorganization of business taxes, while the similar are requested to be removed to avoid harsh burdens. Yesterday, we specially drafted a letter of opinion and sent it to the Executive Committee of our association, asking them to review it and forward it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for approval to the authorities. Now, we are copying the draft and sending it to the cars to draft, and notify our association to jointly present it, in order to receive the effect of joint efforts, still tell to be restored, this to Mr. Zhang Dalian, Chairman of the Shanghai Soy Sauce and Liquor Industry Association, Shanghai Tobacco and Exchange Industry Association Shanghai South Office Kai 19 · 12 · 10 ·

Foreign Merchants Falsely Accuse National Goods of Being Counterfeit 156

Yonghe Toothpaste Confiscated by Customs in Rangoon

Cosmetics Association Asks the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Strive for Justice

The Shanghai Cosmetics Industry Association received a letter from its member, Yonghe Industrial Company, reporting that its Moon Goddess brand toothpaste, which was being shipped to Rangoon in Southeast Asia, was falsely accused by the American merchant Colgate Company of having a similar trademark, and it reported it to Rangoon Customs, which confiscated the goods. The association believes that this matter concerns foreign merchants falsely accusing national goods of being counterfeit, and it has sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to argue for justice based on reason. The original letter states: "Dear Sirs, we have recently received a letter from our member, Yonghe Industrial Company, reporting that the Moon Goddess brand toothpaste manufactured by our company was recently shipped to Rangoon in Southeast Asia and was considered by the American merchant Colgate Company to have the same box paper color as the toothpaste products of the company, and the box did not indicate the words "Made in China", so it reported it to Rangoon Customs, which confiscated the goods, so that the consignee cannot pick it up. Trademark disputes are common, but they must be resolved by the local trademark registration agency or the relevant government agency in accordance with the law, and cannot be confiscated based on the opinions of one party. The toothpaste box of our company uses the Moon Goddess trademark, which is completely different from the toothpaste trademark of Colgate Company, and there are Chinese instructions in Western Shanghar, and the words "Made by Yonghe Industrial Company", so the American merchant said that it did not indicate the words "Made in China", which is obviously inconsistent, other text arrangements, color distribution, are also not similar, how can it be regarded as the same, and the customs confiscated it. We have always admired your association and the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce for promoting and maintaining overseas trade with all our strength. Our company has been interfered with by American merchants this time, and the business has suffered a great loss. We implore you to write to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and forward it to the Chinese Consulate in Rangoon, and to argue with the customs in accordance with the law, and to release the confiscated toothpaste immediately." The association is based on the fact that the Moon Goddess brand toothpaste trademark produced by Yonghe Industrial Company is different in shape from the toothpaste trademark produced by the American merchant Colgate Company, and the products of Yonghe Industrial Company are marked with "Made by Yonghe Industrial Company" and "Using this Moon Goddess brand toothpaste to wipe the teeth can remove the dirt from the teeth and make the teeth white, and it will prevent erosion, pain, and falling off, and it will be firm until old." Like this, the American merchant Colgate Company considered it to be similar and suddenly asked Rangoon Customs to confiscate the goods, which is intentionally hindering our country's overseas trade. We are sending this letter to you to ask the responsible party to uphold the purpose of maintaining overseas trade and to telegraph the Chinese Consulate and the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Rangoon to argue for justice in accordance with the law and to release the confiscated goods in full to protect commercial rights and maintain commercial transportation. Yours truly, Shanghai Cosmetics Industry Association, December 10, 1919 of the Republic of China.

Tao Agui, a Chinese worker who refueled the Asbeck wheel of the Dutch Rudder Rossetti Shipping Company, fell and injured his knee while on duty, resulting in disability. The upper and lower separation of the broken knee bone can only be buckled with a medicinal thread, which is extremely unstable, and of course it will become disabled, and the medicinal thread does not have black spots attached, which is sufficient to prove that it is not caused by other residual toxins that caused the injury to not heal. The above situation has been filled out by the doctor for certification when and a paper copy of the X-ray photo is taken. However, Tao Agui is disabled and his family is extremely poor. They will not be able to shirk their responsibility. Now, we are sending the Tao Agui who has been re-examined to be injured and non-toxic, together with the certificate and the X-ray photographs, to be submitted to your ministry, and we beg you to check and quickly order the Consul in Amsterdam to seriously negotiate the evidence, and strive to issue the pension to Tao Agui as usual, so as to avoid injustice and to care for the injured worker. What should be done is still waiting for instructions to follow. This is to the National Government Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the Executive Yuan, and a certificate and photo of Tao Agui and a photo of the injured place are submitted. (2) A letter of condolence to the injured seaman Tao Agui, the certificate of the German doctor's verification of the knee injury is non-toxic and the X-ray photos are sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for transfer to the Consul in Amsterdam for serious negotiation and the issuance of pensions. Now send two copies of the original negative, and ask for instructions before proceeding accordingly. This is to Comrade Tao Agui, the Chinese Seamen's Industrial United General Association.

Indians Display Fierce Arrogance 159

A Scene of a Ferocious Drama on a German Ship

Indians Rob Money and Commit Murder

Wang Ada Has No Grievances to Clear

The British Consulate Protects in Bad Faith

Wang Ada, the owner of the Wang Longji Leather Shoe Store in this port, delivered leather shoes to the Fulda merchant ship, the manager of the German firm Meisitzer, which was moored at the Customs No. 12 Buoy in the Hongkou Port, at 5:30 PM on the 7th of this month to collect from the buyer. After the matter was completed, he walked out of the office of the master steward at 7:30 PM. Unexpectedly, Namrozee Khan, an Indian watchman hired by the firm, suddenly blocked his way and demanded compensation (commonly known as drinking money) of two yuan. Wang believed that he was engaged in legitimate business, so why should the watchman extort him unreasonably? He told him that he had no money with him, and then left. The Indian followed him. Wang wanted to walk down the ladder at the back of the ship, but the Indian did not allow it and forced Wang to go down the ladder at the front. Wang did not dare to resist. Just as he stepped on the top ladder, the Indian suddenly grabbed Wang's head and neck from behind with both hands, pressed him to the ground, and pressed his head with his knees and his abdomen with one knee. Wang could not breathe. The Indian tore Wang's pockets and the mouth of his pouch, took out three gold pound notes and ten mark notes, put them in his pocket, and then let go. About three minutes later, Wang woke up and shouted for help, but the ship was in the middle of the Huangpu River, and no one heard it. No one on the ship paid attention to it. Wang went to the upper floor to call for help, but no one came out to ask. Wang had no choice but to see that no one was upholding justice, so he went down again, intending to go ashore and return to the store. Unexpectedly, as soon as he went up the handrail, the Indian grabbed Wang's felt hat. Wang refused to accept it and went back up to grab the hat, but was again beaten severely on the head and around the eyes by the Indian. Wang was unable to describe it reasonably for a while and could only endure it and take a boat to shore. That night, he reported to the water patrol station, asking them to investigate the Indian who committed the murder. The head of the patrol station approved the request and went to the British Consulate the next day (i.e., the 8th) to sign out a warrant to arrest the Indian who committed the murder. He also notified the German firm Meisitzer to immediately inform the Indian to surrender himself, otherwise he would board the ship and arrest him. Upon receiving this news, the Indian surrendered himself to the water patrol station at 9:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 9th). After the head of the patrol station interrogated him briefly, he ordered him to be sent to the Central Police Station of the Public Concession for detention overnight. At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, the head of the patrol station ordered a Western police officer to bring back the Indian who committed the murder and ordered the Chinese detective Wu Rongsheng to bring the plaintiff Wang Ada and the witness Zhu Yulai, the boatman of sampan No. 1030, to the British Consulate to wait for interrogation. He also sent interpreter Gu Caiwen to relay the message. The trial began at 10:00 AM. First, the plaintiff stated the process of the defendant's murder and robbery and presented a doctor's certificate to verify the injury. Then, the witness Zhu Yulai proved that he witnessed the defendant's brutal assault on the plaintiff. According to the defendant's confession, he overturned what the plaintiff had said and refused to admit it. He only claimed that the defendant boarded the ship at about 8:00 PM, and because the time for idlers to board the ship had passed, he prevented the plaintiff from boarding the ship, which led to a quarrel. He completely denied the two incidents of assault and robbery and accused the plaintiff of fabricating them. According to the testimony of the Indian head of the watchmen, it was the same as the defendant's. At 12:00 noon, the trial had not yet been concluded. At 2:00 PM, the questioning officer continued to interrogate the plaintiff and the defendant. After the debate, the questioning officer announced the verdict at 2:15 PM that there was no evidence to support the plaintiff's accusations and the defendant was acquitted. The reason was that the plaintiff's eyes were swollen and bruised from the beating and his pockets were torn, and he did not report it to the patrol station until the next day. Ada was unable to defend himself at this point and could only shout for injustice and come out.

Provincial Party Department Investigators Arrest Communists 160

For failing to notify the police precinct first,

Qu Yousheng accused them of extortion.

After investigation, they were declared not guilty.

Qu had previously committed robbery.

Fang Guozhen of Jiangyin, an investigator from the Organization Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department, recently reported to the Provincial Party Department that Qu Yousheng of Qingjiang, an internal medicine doctor residing at No. 846 Maigen Lane, Maigen Road, Shanghai Public Concession, was a Communist. Therefore, he reported it. The Provincial Party Department immediately informed the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, which in turn informed the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting to jointly apprehend and punish him with the concession police. Director Yuan then sent a letter to the Special District Local Court to issue an arrest warrant. However, before the warrant was issued to the police, Fang Guozhen, together with his men Gao Xitang, Du Jiazhen, Yang Zibao, Shen Sandu, and Mao Fengying, directly knocked on Qu's door at 6:15 AM the other morning and broke in. They dragged Qu to a small teahouse at No. 802 nearby and made demands. Qu's wife, Mrs. Zhang, after her husband was dragged out by the crowd and not returning by 11:00 AM, went to the Gordon Road Police Precinct to report Fang and others for extortion. The police chief then ordered detectives to take Fang and the six others, including Qu, to the police precinct for detention. Yesterday, they were sent to the Special Court, where Judge Wu interrogated them. The police lawyer, Tu Yaotang, stated that the defendants were being prosecuted for two crimes: obstructing the freedom of others under Article 316 of the Criminal Code and extortion under Article 370. He also described the defendants' actions at the time, stating that Fang led the crowd into Qu's house and said to Qu, "You are suspected of being a reactionary, and the court has now issued a warrant. If you can pay 100 yuan, you may be able to avoid arrest." Qu only gave them ten yuan and was dragged to a small teahouse for negotiation. Later, the police received a report and went to arrest them. Subsequently, Mr. and Mrs. Qu explained the situation, questioning Fang's statement. Fang confessed that he had known Qu for a long time and knew that he was a Communist, so he reported him. At 7:45 AM yesterday morning, he went to Qu's house alone to observe his movements and invited Qu to the small teahouse, ordering his assistants to guard him. He then went to the Public Security Bureau to report. He only did not understand the concession regulations and did not notify the police precinct first, and did not extort him. The other five people all said that they were helping because Fang asked them to, and they knew nothing else. After questioning, Judge Wu immediately ruled that Fang Guozhen and the other six were not guilty. Within the appeal period, they each paid a surety to be available when summoned. Qu Yousheng was reported to have Communist suspicions, and the court had issued a warrant. Therefore, the police immediately detained Qu. However, after investigation, it was found that Qu was indeed not a good person. Years ago, he was sentenced to six months in prison by the former Mixed Court for theft and was expelled from the concession after serving his sentence. After Judge Wu concluded the case against Fang and others, he continued to bring Qu to court for trial. The police lawyer did not recognize Qu as a resident of the concession because he had been expelled from the concession before and had no objections to the Public Security Bureau's transfer. Judge Wu then questioned Qu and ordered the officers from the Municipal Public Security Bureau to take him away for verification.

Tide Rises, Boat Sinks 162

Zhang Linfa's boat from Songjiang

Zhang Linfa, a Songjiang boatman selling rice, recently collected 140 shi of new rice in the Zhangyan area and transported it to Shanghai, entrusting it to the rice merchant Qian to sell on consignment. The boat sailed to Shanghai the other day and berthed at the special wharf for rice merchants in Xuejia浜. At that time, the tide was low, and the boat was moored below the wharf. Zhang left the boat and went ashore, leaving only two crew members to guard the boat. However, at noon the other day, when the tide rose sharply, the boat gradually floated up. However, when the tide rose enough, the boat was blocked and stuck under the wharf and could not float, causing it to be flooded by the tide. The crew members guarding the boat saw this and tried to push the boat away from the wharf, but it was too late. The boat sank, and the two crew members also fell into the water. Fortunately, it was daytime, and they were not drowned. They were rescued by neighboring boats. When the tide receded, Zhang tried to raise the boat. Much of the rice in the boat floated away, and the rice in the boat was all wet. The oars, poles, and boat equipment also floated away. Zhang immediately reported to the rice merchant Qian, who sold the wet rice on the boat to the sugar factory for cooking sugar for only four yuan and a few cents per stone. The losses were estimated to be very large.

Zhang San's boat from Jiangbei

Zhang San, a boatman from Jiangbei, recently transported firewood from Jiangbei to Shanghai to sell through a firm. He arrived in Shanghai the afternoon before yesterday and berthed on the south side of the Datong Wharf in the South City. At 12:00 PM, the Zhengzhou steamer of the Haizhou class of the United Company entered the port and berthed next to the Datong Wharf. At that time, the tide was rising rapidly, and it crashed into Zhang's boat's bow with the current, shattering it. The tide flooded in, and the boat sank. Zhang and the crew members were all sleeping in the stern. When they saw the water flooding the cabin, they ran out and shouted for help. Because it was late at night, there were no boats to rescue them. Fortunately, Zhang and others were familiar with the water and floated to the shore, where they were rescued by a boat. Only the hull of Zhang's boat remained, floating on the water. All the firewood in the boat floated away. Zhang is now negotiating with the shipping company to claim compensation for the losses.

Municipal Government Bans Broken Boats and Pile Driving, Obstructing Waterways 165

The Third District Party Department of this city, according to the report from the Fifteenth District Branch, stated that along the banks of the Suzhou River in the Caojiadu area, broken boats from Jiangbei have been moored for a long time without leaving. Some even drive wooden piles,擱起the boats, and intend to stay for a long time. Among them, men and women are factory workers or peddlers, not boatmen, and occupying the waterfront is already wrong. Moreover, driving piles and long-term mooring slows the river flow, causing siltation over time. Residents along the banks will then encroach on the river beach and build houses because of this. Broken boats will then live by the houses, and after a long time, they will become houses again. The waterway is being eroded day by day, and traffic will be blocked. Abandoned Her Husband and Disowned Her Father 172

A Woman's Heart Cannot Be Measured

An Old Father Wants to Get Her Back at Any Cost

Wu Dazhangzi, a 29-year-old woman from Yancheng, is the daughter of Wu Yiming, who lives at No. 20 Hengjie Street, Puyutang. She used to be married to Luo Wenxue, a rickshaw puller. Because she could not endure poverty, she became acquainted with Zhou Yaojun from Guangdong. She then found a way to separate from her husband. Although separated, Wu Yiming still wanted to restrain his daughter and seek the right to arrange her marriage again. However, his daughter did not want her lover to spend money, so she severed ties with her father. Wu was furious and went out to search everywhere, vowing to vent his anger. Yesterday, he met Zhou in Wangjialong, South City, and arrested him. He was transferred to the local court by the First Section of the First Precinct for trial.

Wife Asks to Divorce Her Husband 173

Judge's Mediation Ineffective

Yao A'bao, a woman from Songjiang, recently hired Lawyer Chen Wen to file a lawsuit in the local court against Zhang Zhangsheng for being unbearable to live with. She requested a divorce and asked for 2,400 yuan in alimony. The defendant Zhang Zhangsheng also hired Lawyer Zhou Yu to file a defense. Yesterday morning, Court President Guo Shouyi opened the court for trial. Both parties arrived in court with their lawyers. First, the plaintiff Yao A'bao, 22 years old, from Songjiang, testified that she used to work as a maid at the Cai family on Kangti Road and is now working at No. 534 Defeng 里, Beijing Road. In 1927, I was only 19 years old. In May of that year, I met the defendant and lived together in Shouxian里, Ximen. Later, I had a child. At this time, the defendant explained to me that he still had a wife at home, so I moved back to my home in Xiaonanmen and lived with his wife. On the sixth day of the first month of this year, the child died of illness. The defendant then quarreled with me, so I left in May and returned to my old job, working as a maid to make a living. But I only worked for three months and resigned due to illness. Because I thought that I would have no one to rely on when I was old, I requested to be allowed to divorce and requested to be given ten years of alimony, calculated at 20 yuan per month, totaling 2,400 yuan. I requested a one-time payment. Next, the defendant Zhang Zhangsheng, 47 years old, a carpenter, testified that in 1927, he took the plaintiff as his concubine. After she gave birth last year, he moved her back to his home to live with him. This time, the plaintiff left for no reason, and I do not want to divorce. The examining official said that it would be better to separate from his wife and pay the plaintiff 20 yuan per month for living expenses. The defendant listened and nodded. The examining official asked the plaintiff again, but she insisted on divorce. Therefore, the mediation failed and the debate began. The lawyers of both parties filed lawsuits against each other. The examining official concluded the debate and scheduled the judgment for the 13th of this month.

Engagement of Surveying Student Terminated 174

In addition to Returning Gold Jewelry,

Compensation of 25 Yuan

Han Zhiqing, a surveying student from the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau, hired Lawyer Wang Jishi to file a lawsuit in the local court requesting to maintain the engagement. The defendant, Ye Maoxi (also known as Fengming), is a staff member of Qingjietang and also hired Lawyer Yao Jian to file a defense, stating that his granddaughter Ye Lijuan opposed this marriage and did not obtain her consent. He also accused the plaintiff of having syphilis. The court had opened a trial and ordered both parties to reconcile outside the court. If the reconciliation failed, the defendant would be ordered to pay the expenses and send the plaintiff to the hospital for an examination to determine whether he had syphilis and ordered the defendant to bring his granddaughter Ye Lijuan to court to wait for questioning. All of this has been reported in the previous report. Yesterday morning, Court President Guo Shouyi continued the trial. First, the defendant's lawyer stated that the case had been reconciled outside the court. All the gold jewelry had been returned to the plaintiff. Regarding the loss issue, the defendant only agreed to compensate the plaintiff 10 yuan, while the plaintiff demanded 40 yuan, so it had not been completely resolved. The examining official ordered both the plaintiff and defendant to the case, questioned them briefly, and then made a decision, ordering the defendant to return the gold jewelry and compensate the plaintiff 25 yuan. The engagement was allowed to be terminated. Both parties were satisfied, so the reconciliation was established. Court President Guo then wrote the reconciliation record and ordered both parties and their lawyers to sign and leave the court.

Husband in Custody, Wife Drowns 175

Wife Dies Without Rescue

Husband Launches Major Negotiation

Yin Zhenggao, a rickshaw puller from Xinghua, at No. 40 Jiangyin Street, Shajia Street, outside the Dananmen, had an argument with his second landlord, Qian Tonglin, and his son, Qian Hongzi, on the 7th of this month. Yin went to mediate and was also beaten. The patrol police arrested Qian and his son and Yin and sent them to the Second District Police Station. As a result, Qian and his son were released, while Yin was detained for five days. Unexpectedly, a tragedy occurred during the detention. After Yin was detained, Yin's wife, Gu (32 years old), questioned Qian and his son and started a conflict, but was insulted and scolded. The woman was filled with anger and her husband was not released, so she went to a nearby stream and committed suicide by drowning. She was rescued, but she had swallowed a lot of water, and it was sewage, which was difficult to vomit out. She was barely breathing. The patrol police reported to the Second District Police Station and released Yin, ordering him to go home to rescue her. He carried his wife home, but she died soon after. Yin was greatly saddened and arrested Qian Tonglin and filed a complaint with the Second District Police Station. They were sent to the court. After interrogation, it was decided to wait for an autopsy and then verify.

Poor Son-in-Law Arrests Father-in-Law to Demand His Wife 176

Zhou Yaojun, a 27-year-old from Guangdong, used to run a cigarette and paper shop outside the Xiaoximen, Nanshi, on Guohuo Road. Three years ago, he married Wu Yiming, a woman from Yancheng, through a matchmaker. The couple's relationship was not bad after Wu came to the door. However, Zhou's business has been declining recently, and all his capital has been lost. Zhou had no choice but to sell the shop and property to a friend in May of this year and move to the French Concession. He then asked his friends to help him find a place to live, but he could not find one for a long time, and his life became more and more difficult. Wu could not bear the poverty of her husband's family, so she secretly slipped out without Zhou's knowledge last month and disappeared. When Zhou realized it, he searched everywhere, but found nothing. Recently, someone secretly told him that Wu's escape was purely instigated by her father, Wu Yiming. Zhou was furious and went to his father-in-law's house at No. 20 Nanmatou yesterday afternoon at about 6:00 PM and arrested Wu Yiming. He then called Gao Diankui, the guard at the 19th post there, and brought him to the First Section of the First Precinct. After the director of the precinct made a preliminary trial, he decided that the matter was related to criminal prosecution and ordered it to be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for trial.

Opium on the Dalian Ship 177

One Sack of More Than Two Hundred and Eighty Taels

Yang Bingkui, the patrol chief of the Water Patrol Team of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, led his team members, including Chuan Yu, to patrol the river to the tenth wharf of Dachang on the 16th yesterday afternoon at about 1:00 PM. The police saw the Dalian ship moored there and about to set sail, so they boarded the ship to conduct an inspection. They found a sack in the cabin, and after opening it, they found opium inside, estimated to be more than 280 taels. The team took the cabin attendant, Huang Xixiong, along with the opium to the team. During the preliminary trial by the team leader Xu, Huang, 37 years old, from Chongming, confessed that the sack had just been thrown into the cabin by a guest when he saw the police team coming. He was ordered to prepare a document and report it to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for trial.

Hengyuan New Rice Store's Tenth Anniversary 179

Hengyuan New Rice Store on An'nan Road in the Public Concession has been open for many years, specializing in the sale of machine-milled white rice, miscellaneous grains, and horse feed from various provinces, managing Hua Yang flour, and offering retail and wholesale prices that are fairer than others. This year is a good harvest, and new products are旺登. The store is celebrating its tenth anniversary and is sparing no expense to purchase and transport products from the production area. The cost is light, and the price is naturally cheap. From December 10th, the store will hold a big sale for three weeks. Residents from near and far see that the store's goods are beautiful and the price is low, and they flock to buy rice. As a result, the store was extremely crowded on the first day yesterday, and the staff was overwhelmed and extremely busy. The store sold more than 1,000 stone of rice all day.

Report on the Jishi Welfare Society of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Beijing Congee Factory 181

The Chinese Jishi Welfare Society set up four congee factories this winter because there are more poor people in Beijing this winter and the current situation is miserable. One of the factories outside Chaoyangmen is managed by Director Bao Jun. The following is its method and the latest situation of congee distribution. The factory director has two managers, and there are two supervisors during congee distribution. According to the report from the end of last month, the number of poor people living in the factory who are old and inconvenient to walk is 61 men and women. The number of people who come to the factory to receive congee every day is 2,050 men and women, and 603 boys and girls, totaling an average of about 2,600 people per day. There are already so many people at the beginning of the office, and there will definitely be a continuous increase in the future. It is necessary to use 561 pounds of millet and 400 pounds of coal every day. People from all walks of life in the Beijing military and government and charitable people come to the factory to visit every day. It is said that the association, for the sake of being practical and realistic, orders the congee factory to send a report form of the poor people living in the factory and a report form of the people who come to the factory to eat every day, one copy each, and send them to the General Association at any time for assessment.

Jiangxi Public Cemetery Begins Tomb Construction 184

The Jiangxi Public Cemetery, run by the Shanghai Jiangxi Guild Hall, is located in the Xuchang Bridge area. Tongyuan Pawnshop Seeks to Protect the Interests of its Customers 185

Moving Ornaments to Shanghai for Storage

The Tongyuan Pawnshop in Ji Hang Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, has recently experienced frequent robberies in the surrounding areas of Punan County. To avoid danger, pawned ornaments are being moved to Shanghai for storage. If someone comes to redeem them, they can come to Shanghai to retrieve them and receive the items after confirmation. Fearing that ignorant people might use this as an excuse to cause trouble, a letter was sent through the Ji Hang Chamber of Commerce requesting the county government to issue a public notice. The county government, after receiving the request, approved the issuance of a notice yesterday to be posted at the pawnshop, so that everyone is aware.

Weather Report 188

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the Yangtze River Basin is cloudy with rain and fog due to a low pressure forming in Jiangxi. There are cyclones in Shandong and the Yangtze River Basin, and the wind direction is uncertain along the coast of the country, with occasional fog in some areas. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 57.0 degrees and the lowest was 38.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 55.2 and the lowest was 44.6.

Received

A Review of the Industrial and Commercial Conference and its Hopes (Continued) by Mu Xiangyue 189

At this conference, the various proposals regarding economic construction generally had considerable decisions that were suitable for the current national conditions and sufficient for the government to adopt. However, upon examining the proposals, most of them were based on discussions and lacked numerical indications. The so-called numerical indications refer to a precise statistic of various industries and commerce in the country. This precise statistic should be automatically investigated by various industries nationwide, and the government should only be responsible for compiling and summarizing the results to provide guidance and protection for various industries nationwide. Our country's industries and commerce have never had this kind of work. Even if someone proposes this matter, various industries would keep it a secret. Although there are wise people, they cannot do anything about it. However, they do not know that at this time, industries and commerce should pay attention to domestic trade everywhere and must deeply understand the trends of industries and commerce in various countries to be able to welcome or reject them appropriately. Without precise statistics, the government cannot fulfill its responsibility of guiding and protecting. At this conference, it was clear that many proposals needed precise statistics as the basis for research, but due to a lack of accurate materials, there was no way to start. All the delegates attending this conference had this feeling, but how to handle the investigation and statistics should also be discussed. Now, let's list an item for cotton industry investigation:

(1) Planting location and quantity (2) Quality

(3) Purchase method (4) Transportation situation

(5) Concentration location (6) Various taxes

(7) Export port (8) Accumulated malpractices and elimination methods

(9) Foreign situation (10) Competitive situation

(11) Methods of developing the industry

All of the above investigations should be carried out by people with knowledge and experience in the industry to make a precise statistic. It is especially important to pay attention to the foreign situation and competitive situation. All industries in the country should make every effort to engage in this statistic. For example, in the match industry, all raw materials, such as phosphorus, wood, box manufacturing, and printing paper, whether the raw materials are produced in the country, if there is a considerable amount of production, what are the prices in each producing area, what are the freight taxes, how is the quality compared to imported products, how is the cost compared to imported products, what is the production volume in each place, how many factories are there in each place, and how many sales are there in each place, all must have accurate numbers as the basis for research and development. Our country's industries and commerce have a wide variety of products. According to the group table of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce Research Association, they are roughly as follows:

Silk Industry Group Cotton Industry Group Rice Industry Group

Timber Industry Group Oil Industry Group Silver Money Industry Group

Exchange Industry Group Iron Industry Group Tea Industry Group

Wool Weaving Industry Group Knitting Industry Group Hemp Industry Group

Paper Industry Group Cigarette Industry Group Match Industry Group

Porcelain Industry Group Coal Group Sugar Industry Group

Brick Tile Lime Industry Group Leather Industry Group Electrical Industry Group

Printing Industry Group Car Manufacturing Industry Group

The above groups only need to select one or two people from the industry to specialize in the investigation business, and then the statistics of each industry will be clearly available. I think that our country's industries and commerce originally have trade associations, so they can seek the development of the industry and gather to discuss matters. The method is excellent. Now, we can expand this method. The various industries can gather the same industries from all over the country to organize a joint association of each industry, hire experts to conduct thorough investigations, which is the simplest and most complete way. In recent years, the Yarn Factory Association has handled statistics with definite results. It is hoped that all industries and commerce in the country will follow suit. After a few years, it will definitely have a great effect. As for the proposals in this conference, such as Mr. Chen Zongcheng's labor investigation statistics, item 3 in Mr. Bian Shousun's relief industry proposal, and the Ministry's industry and commerce visiting bureau requesting the handling of regional investigations of national industry and commerce, all pay attention to industrial statistics. For example, the labor statistics item is already being undertaken by the government, so we can ignore it for now. Mr. Bian and the visiting bureau proposed requesting the government to investigate to promote national production and to conduct regional investigations of national industry and commerce. The planning is very appropriate, but it is still difficult for the government to handle it alone. (1) There is no economic way to handle it, because large-scale investigations cannot be done without setting up bureaus in different regions. At this time of financial constraints, how can this huge amount of funds be raised? (2) There is no way to concentrate talents. Various industries and commerce have their own specialties. The silk industry does not know the way of the sugar industry, and the rice industry does not know the reason of the tea industry. If the government handles it, it will be impossible to concentrate so many talents. (3) The old habits of our country's industries and commerce make it difficult for outsiders to discover the bottom line. Even if someone engages in investigations, non-industry people will find it difficult to get the truth. (4) Our country has a vast territory and abundant resources. The industries and commerce, such as the 23 groups listed above, may not be able to cover all of them. If the government is solely responsible for the investigation, it may lead to omissions, and it will not be possible to complete the task in a short period of time. All of these points should be noted. I think that the national industrial and commercial survey should be the responsibility of each industry, and the government should summarize the results. Therefore, there must first be accurate statistics from each industry's own investigation, and then the government will have a solid basis. The government can find ways to eliminate what is harmful to each industry, and the government can do its best to develop what is beneficial to each industry. Only in this way can the national economic construction proceed step by step to fulfill the mission of the Three Principles of the People. This is the reason why I advocate that national industrial and commercial statistics should be automatically investigated by each industry. It is hoped that the national industrial and commercial circles will rise up and plan for it.

Wedding Announcement 192

Mr. Wang Shizhen, a teacher at Youth Middle School, and Ms. Zhang Yunhua were married on November 24th at Nantong Central Park. Last night, a banquet was held at the Tongxing Building to entertain relatives and friends in Shanghai. The guests joked and teased at will, and the room was filled with witty words, which was quite a grand occasion. It is reported that Ms. Zhang is currently working part-time at the Municipal Yude Elementary School.

Art and Calligraphy News 193

Yesterday was the seventh day of the art exhibition of Mr. Wang Yachen and his wife Rong, which happened to be a Sunday, and the viewers were even more enthusiastic. In addition to the artists and art school students from Shanghai who came one after another, there were also many Western and Japanese viewers. In such a good venue, with systematic research displayed, plus the neat arrangement and novel easels, a tour of the entire venue is like traveling in Western Europe. In addition to Mr. Wang and Mr. Rong personally interacting with the visitors, there are also students from the Xinhua Art School and art friends of the two gentlemen, who are warmly welcoming them. It can be called an unprecedented art exhibition in Shanghai.

Publishing News 194

The Jingwu Association on North Sichuan Road announced that Mr. Xue Gongchu, a martial arts expert, has written a book entitled "Guidelines for Combat," which divides the content into four major sections: boxing techniques, weapons, theory, and boxing scores. It describes in detail the methods of practicing, applying, common mistakes, and various key points of Chinese martial arts. It is truly an unprecedented masterpiece in the martial arts world. It has now been published and handed over to the association for sale.
